        @if (lifeCycleEvents.Count == 0)
        {
            <p class="text-muted">Esta herramienta aún no tiene eventos registrados.</p>
        }
        else
        {
            <div class="timeline">
                @foreach (var item in lifeCycleEvents.OrderByDescending(x => x.EventDate))
                {
                    <div class="timeline-item">
                        <div class="timeline-dot"></div>

                        <div class="timeline-content">
                            <div class="timeline-header">
                                <strong>@item.Title</strong>
                                <span>@item.EventDate.ToLocalTime().ToString("dd/MM/yyyy HH:mm")</span>
                            </div>

                            <small class="text-muted">@item.EventType</small>

                            @if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(item.Description))
                            {
                                <p>@item.Description</p>
                            }

                            <div class="timeline-values">
                                <span>Anterior: @ShowValue(item.PreviousValue)</span>
                                <span>Nuevo: @ShowValue(item.NewValue)</span>
                                <span>Usuario: @ShowValue(item.PerformedBy)</span>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                }
            </div>
        }
    </section>
}

@code {
    [Parameter]
    public Guid ToolId { get; set; }

    private bool isLoading;
    private bool isSaving;
    private string? actionMessage;
    private string selectedOperationalStatus = "PendingValidation";
    private string actionObservation = string.Empty;
    private string? errorMessage;
    private ToolDetailItem? tool;
    private List<LifeCycleEventItem> lifeCycleEvents = new();

    protected override async Task OnInitializedAsync()
    {
        await LoadAsync();
    }

    private async Task LoadAsync()
    {
        try
        {
            isLoading = true;
            errorMessage = null;

            var client = HttpClientFactory.CreateClient("NaviApi");

            tool = await client.GetFromJsonAsync<ToolDetailItem>($"api/tools/{ToolId}");

            if (tool is not null)
            {
                selectedOperationalStatus = tool!.OperationalStatus;
            }
            lifeCycleEvents = await client.GetFromJsonAsync<List<LifeCycleEventItem>>($"api/tools/{ToolId}/life-cycle-events") ?? new();
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            errorMessage = $"No se pudo cargar el detalle. Valida que la API esté activa en http://localhost:5218. Detalle: {ex.Message}";
        }
        finally
        {
            isLoading = false;
        }
    }

    private async Task ChangeOperationalStatusAsync()
    {
        if (tool is null)
        {
            return;
        }

        try
        {
            isSaving = true;
            actionMessage = null;
            errorMessage = null;

            var client = HttpClientFactory.CreateClient("NaviApi");

            var payload = new
            {
                operationalStatus = selectedOperationalStatus,
                changedBy = "yquinto",
                updatedBy = "yquinto",
                reason = actionObservation,
                observation = actionObservation
            };

            var response = await client.PatchAsJsonAsync($"api/tools/{tool.Id}/operational-status", payload);

            if (!response.IsSuccessStatusCode)
            {
                var detail = await response.Content.ReadAsStringAsync();
                errorMessage = $"No se pudo cambiar el estado. Código: {(int)response.StatusCode}. Detalle: {detail}";
                return;
            }

            actionMessage = "Estado operativo actualizado correctamente.";
            actionObservation = string.Empty;

            await LoadAsync();
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            errorMessage = $"No se pudo cambiar el estado. Detalle: {ex.Message}";
        }
        finally
        {
            isSaving = false;
        }
    }

    private async Task ToggleSpecializedAsync()
    {
        if (tool is null)
        {
            return;
        }

        try
        {
            isSaving = true;
            actionMessage = null;
            errorMessage = null;

            var client = HttpClientFactory.CreateClient("NaviApi");

            var payload = new
            {
                isSpecialized = !tool.IsSpecialized,
                changedBy = "yquinto",
                updatedBy = "yquinto",
                reason = "Cambio de clasificación desde Admin."
            };

            var response = await client.PatchAsJsonAsync($"api/tools/{tool.Id}/classification", payload);

            if (!response.IsSuccessStatusCode)
            {
                var detail = await response.Content.ReadAsStringAsync();
                errorMessage = $"No se pudo cambiar la clasificación. Código: {(int)response.StatusCode}. Detalle: {detail}";
                return;
            }

            actionMessage = "Clasificación actualizada correctamente.";

            await LoadAsync();
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            errorMessage = $"No se pudo cambiar la clasificación. Detalle: {ex.Message}";
        }
        finally
        {
            isSaving = false;
        }
    }
    private void GoBack()
    {
        NavigationManager.NavigateTo("/tools");
    }

    private static string ShowValue(string? value)
    {
        return string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(value) ? "-" : value;
    }

    private static string BoolLabel(bool value)
    {
        return value ? "Sí" : "No";
    }

    private static string FormatDate(DateTime? value)
    {
        return value.HasValue ? value.Value.ToString("dd/MM/yyyy") : "-";
    }

    private static string GetStatusLabel(string? status)
    {
        return status switch
        {
            "Available" => "Disponible",
            "Assigned" => "Asignada",
            "Loaned" => "Prestada",
            "InMaintenance" => "En mantenimiento",
            "Damaged" => "Dańada",
            "NotSuitable" => "No apta",
            "PendingValidation" => "Pendiente validación",
            "Inconsistent" => "Inconsistente",
            "NotLocated" => "No localizada",
            "PendingDisposal" => "Pendiente de baja",
            "Disposed" => "Dada de baja",
            _ => string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(status) ? "Sin estado" : status
        };
    }

    private static string GetStatusBadgeClass(string? status)
    {
        return status switch
        {
            "Available" => "badge bg-success",
            "PendingValidation" => "badge bg-warning text-dark",
            "Loaned" => "badge bg-info text-dark",
            "InMaintenance" => "badge bg-primary",
            "Damaged" => "badge bg-danger",
            "NotSuitable" => "badge bg-danger",
            "NotLocated" => "badge bg-dark",
            "Inconsistent" => "badge bg-danger",
            "Disposed" => "badge bg-secondary",
            _ => "badge bg-secondary"
        };
    }

    private sealed class ToolDetailItem
    {
        public Guid Id { get; set; }
        public string InternalCode { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string Name { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string? Description { get; set; }
        public string? Brand { get; set; }
        public string? Model { get; set; }
        public string? SerialNumber { get; set; }
        public string? FixedAssetCode { get; set; }
        public string? FenixCode { get; set; }
        public string? UnitOfMeasure { get; set; }
        public decimal Quantity { get; set; }
        public bool IsSpecialized { get; set; }
        public bool RequiresMaintenance { get; set; }
        public bool RequiresPreOperationalCheck { get; set; }
        public bool RequiresCertification { get; set; }
        public DateTime? CertificationExpirationDate { get; set; }
        public string? BranchCode { get; set; }
        public string? BranchName { get; set; }
        public string? LocationCode { get; set; }
        public string? LocationName { get; set; }
        public string? ResponsiblePersonName { get; set; }
        public string? ToolTypeCode { get; set; }
        public string? ToolTypeName { get; set; }
        public string? ToolCategoryCode { get; set; }
        public string? ToolCategoryName { get; set; }
        public string OperationalStatus { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string PhysicalStatus { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string CustodyStatus { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string ReconciliationStatus { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string SyncStatus { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    }

    private sealed class LifeCycleEventItem
    {
        public Guid Id { get; set; }
        public Guid ToolAssetId { get; set; }
        public string EventType { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string Title { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string? Description { get; set; }
        public string? PreviousValue { get; set; }
        public string? NewValue { get; set; }
        public DateTime EventDate { get; set; }
        public string? PerformedBy { get; set; }
    }
}

                            <th>Fecha</th>
                            <th>Evento</th>
                            <th>Título</th>
                            <th>Anterior</th>
                            <th>Nuevo</th>
                            <th>Usuario</th>
                        </tr>
                    </thead>
                    <tbody>
                        @foreach (var item in record.LifeCycleEvents)
                        {
                            <tr>
                                <td>@DateTimeText(item.EventDate)</td>
                                <td>@item.EventType</td>
                                <td>@item.Title</td>
                                <td>@Show(item.PreviousValue)</td>
                                <td>@Show(item.NewValue)</td>
                                <td>@Show(item.PerformedBy)</td>
                            </tr>
                        }
                    </tbody>
                </table>
            </div>
        }
    </section>
}

@code {
    private string GetMaintenanceAlertClass()
    {
        var days = GetDaysUntilNextMaintenance();

        if (!days.HasValue)
        {
            return "maintenance-alert maintenance-alert-neutral";
        }

        if (days.Value < 0)
        {
            return "maintenance-alert maintenance-alert-danger";
        }

        if (days.Value <= 30)
        {
            return "maintenance-alert maintenance-alert-warning";
        }

        return "maintenance-alert maintenance-alert-success";
    }

    private string GetMaintenanceAlertTitle()
    {
        var days = GetDaysUntilNextMaintenance();

        if (!days.HasValue)
        {
            return "Sin fecha programada";
        }

        if (days.Value < 0)
        {
            return "Mantenimiento vencido";
        }

        if (days.Value <= 30)
        {
            return "Mantenimiento próximo";
        }

        return "Mantenimiento al día";
    }

    private string GetMaintenanceAlertDescription()
    {
        var days = GetDaysUntilNextMaintenance();

        if (!days.HasValue)
        {
            return "La herramienta no tiene una fecha de próximo mantenimiento registrada.";
        }

        if (days.Value < 0)
        {
            return $"El mantenimiento está vencido hace {Math.Abs(days.Value)} día(s).";
        }

        if (days.Value == 0)
        {
            return "El mantenimiento está programado para hoy.";
        }

        if (days.Value <= 30)
        {
            return $"El mantenimiento está próximo. Faltan {days.Value} día(s).";
        }

        return $"La herramienta se encuentra al día. Faltan {days.Value} día(s) para el próximo mantenimiento.";
    }

    private string GetMaintenanceDaysText()
    {
        var days = GetDaysUntilNextMaintenance();

        if (!days.HasValue)
        {
            return "-";
        }

        return days.Value < 0
            ? $"Vencido {Math.Abs(days.Value)} día(s)"
            : $"{days.Value} día(s)";
    }

    private int? GetDaysUntilNextMaintenance()
    {
        if (record?.MaintenancePlan?.NextMaintenanceDate is null)
        {
            return null;
        }

        var next = record.MaintenancePlan.NextMaintenanceDate.Value.Date;
        var today = DateTime.Today;

        return (next - today).Days;
    }

    private static string ShowDate(DateTime? value)
    {
        return value.HasValue
            ? value.Value.ToString("dd/MM/yyyy")
            : "-";
    }

    [Parameter]
    public Guid ToolId { get; set; }

    private bool isLoading;
    private string? errorMessage;
    private TechnicalLifeRecordModel? record;

    protected override async Task OnInitializedAsync()
    {
        await LoadAsync();
    }

    private async Task LoadAsync()
    {
        try
        {
            isLoading = true;
            errorMessage = null;

            var client = HttpClientFactory.CreateClient("NaviApi");

            record = await client.GetFromJsonAsync<TechnicalLifeRecordModel>($"api/tools/{ToolId}/technical-life-record");
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            errorMessage = $"No se pudo cargar la hoja de vida técnica. Valida que la API esté activa en http://localhost:5218. Detalle: {ex.Message}";
        }
        finally
        {
            isLoading = false;
        }
    }

    private void GoBack()
    {
        NavigationManager.NavigateTo("/tools");
    }

    private string BuildApiUrl(string? relativeUrl)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(relativeUrl))
        {
            return "#";
        }

        if (relativeUrl.StartsWith("http", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
        {
            return relativeUrl;
        }

        var baseUrl = Configuration["NaviApi:BaseUrl"] ?? "http://localhost:5218";

        return $"{baseUrl.TrimEnd('/')}/{relativeUrl.TrimStart('/')}";
    }

    private async Task PrintLifeRecord()
    {
        await JsRuntime.InvokeVoidAsync("window.print");
    }

    private static string Show(string? value)
    {
        return string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(value) ? "-" : value;
    }

    private static string NumberText(int? value)
    {
        return value.HasValue ? value.Value.ToString() : "-";
    }

    private static string BoolText(bool? value)
    {
        return value.HasValue ? BoolText(value.Value) : "-";
    }

    private static string BoolText(bool value)
    {
        return value ? "Sí" : "No";
    }

    private static string DateText(DateTime? value)
    {
        return value.HasValue ? value.Value.ToString("dd/MM/yyyy") : "-";
    }

    private static string DateTimeText(DateTime? value)
    {
        return value.HasValue ? value.Value.ToLocalTime().ToString("dd/MM/yyyy HH:mm") : "-";
    }

    private static int GetPercent(int? value)
    {
        return Math.Clamp(value ?? 0, 0, 100);
    }

    private static string GetStatusLabel(string? status)
    {
        return status switch
        {
            "Available" => "Disponible",
            "Assigned" => "Asignada",
            "Loaned" => "Prestada",
            "InMaintenance" => "En mantenimiento",
            "Damaged" => "Dańada",
            "NotSuitable" => "No apta",
            "PendingValidation" => "Pendiente validación",
            "Inconsistent" => "Inconsistente",
            "NotLocated" => "No localizada",
            "PendingDisposal" => "Pendiente de baja",
            "Disposed" => "Dada de baja",
            _ => string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(status) ? "Sin estado" : status
        };
    }

    private static string GetStatusBadgeClass(string? status)
    {
        return status switch
        {
            "Available" => "badge bg-success",
            "PendingValidation" => "badge bg-warning text-dark",
            "Loaned" => "badge bg-info text-dark",
            "InMaintenance" => "badge bg-primary",
            "Damaged" => "badge bg-danger",
            "NotSuitable" => "badge bg-danger",
            "NotLocated" => "badge bg-dark",
            "Inconsistent" => "badge bg-danger",
            "Disposed" => "badge bg-secondary",
            _ => "badge bg-secondary"
        };
    }

@code {
    [Parameter]
    public Guid ToolId { get; set; }

    private bool isLoading;
    private bool isSaving;
    private string? errorMessage;
    private string? successMessage;
    private string internalCode = string.Empty;
    private string toolName = string.Empty;
    private TechnicalEditModel? editModel;

    protected override async Task OnInitializedAsync()
    {
        await LoadAsync();
    }

    private async Task LoadAsync()
    {
        try
        {
            isLoading = true;
            errorMessage = null;
            successMessage = null;

            var client = HttpClientFactory.CreateClient("NaviApi");

            var record = await client.GetFromJsonAsync<TechnicalLifeRecordForEditModel>($"api/tools/{ToolId}/technical-life-record");

            if (record is null)
            {
                errorMessage = "No se encontró información técnica para la herramienta.";
                return;
            }

            internalCode = record.Summary.InternalCode;
            toolName = record.Summary.Name;

            editModel = new TechnicalEditModel
            {
                Brand = record.EquipmentInformation.Brand,
                Model = record.EquipmentInformation.Model,
                SerialNumber = record.EquipmentInformation.SerialNumber,
                FixedAssetCode = record.EquipmentInformation.FixedAssetCode,
                FenixCode = record.EquipmentInformation.FenixCode,
                AcquisitionDate = record.EquipmentInformation.AcquisitionDate?.Date,

                Voltage = record.TechnicalSpecifications.Voltage,
                LoadCapacity = record.TechnicalSpecifications.LoadCapacity,
                Provider = record.TechnicalSpecifications.Provider,
                RequiresMaintenance = record.TechnicalSpecifications.RequiresMaintenance,
                RequiresPreOperationalCheck = record.TechnicalSpecifications.RequiresPreOperationalCheck,
                RequiresCertification = record.TechnicalSpecifications.RequiresCertification,
                CertificationExpirationDate = record.TechnicalSpecifications.CertificationExpirationDate?.Date,

                HasWarranty = record.Warranty.HasWarranty,
                WarrantyType = record.Warranty.WarrantyType,

                UsefulLifeStartDate = record.UsefulLife.StartDate?.Date,
                UsefulLifeMonths = record.UsefulLife.UsefulLifeMonths,
                UsefulLifeDays = record.UsefulLife.UsefulLifeDays,

                LastMaintenanceDate = record.MaintenancePlan.LastMaintenanceDate?.Date,
                NextMaintenanceDate = record.MaintenancePlan.NextMaintenanceDate?.Date,
                MaintenancePeriodMonths = record.MaintenancePlan.MaintenancePeriodMonths,

                UpdatedBy = "yquinto",
                Observation = "Actualización de datos técnicos desde Admin."
            };
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            errorMessage = $"No se pudo cargar la información técnica. Valida que la API esté activa. Detalle: {ex.Message}";
        }
        finally
        {
            isLoading = false;
        }
    }

    private async Task SaveAsync()
    {
        if (editModel is null)
        {
            return;
        }

        try
        {
            isSaving = true;
            errorMessage = null;
            successMessage = null;

            var client = HttpClientFactory.CreateClient("NaviApi");

            var response = await client.PatchAsJsonAsync($"api/tools/{ToolId}/technical-data", editModel);

            if (!response.IsSuccessStatusCode)
            {
                var detail = await response.Content.ReadAsStringAsync();
                errorMessage = $"No se pudieron actualizar los datos técnicos. Código: {(int)response.StatusCode}. Detalle: {detail}";
                return;
            }

            successMessage = "Datos técnicos actualizados correctamente.";
            await LoadAsync();
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            errorMessage = $"No se pudieron actualizar los datos técnicos. Detalle: {ex.Message}";
        }
        finally
        {
            isSaving = false;
        }
    }

    private void GoBack()
    {
        NavigationManager.NavigateTo($"/tools/{ToolId}/technical-life-record");
    }

    private sealed class TechnicalEditModel
    {
        public string? Brand { get; set; }
        public string? Model { get; set; }
        public string? SerialNumber { get; set; }
        public string? FixedAssetCode { get; set; }
        public string? FenixCode { get; set; }
        public DateTime? AcquisitionDate { get; set; }
        public string? Voltage { get; set; }
        public string? LoadCapacity { get; set; }
        public string? Provider { get; set; }
        public bool HasWarranty { get; set; }
        public string? WarrantyType { get; set; }
        public DateTime? UsefulLifeStartDate { get; set; }
        public int? UsefulLifeMonths { get; set; }
        public int? UsefulLifeDays { get; set; }
        public DateTime? LastMaintenanceDate { get; set; }
        public DateTime? NextMaintenanceDate { get; set; }
        public int? MaintenancePeriodMonths { get; set; }
        public bool RequiresMaintenance { get; set; }
        public bool RequiresPreOperationalCheck { get; set; }
        public bool RequiresCertification { get; set; }
        public DateTime? CertificationExpirationDate { get; set; }
        public string? UpdatedBy { get; set; }
        public string? Observation { get; set; }
    }

    private sealed class TechnicalLifeRecordForEditModel
    {
        public SummaryInfo Summary { get; set; } = new();
        public EquipmentInfo EquipmentInformation { get; set; } = new();
        public TechnicalInfo TechnicalSpecifications { get; set; } = new();
        public WarrantyInfo Warranty { get; set; } = new();
        public UsefulLifeInfo UsefulLife { get; set; } = new();
        public MaintenancePlanInfo MaintenancePlan { get; set; } = new();
    }

    private sealed class SummaryInfo
    {
        public string InternalCode { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string Name { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    }

    private sealed class EquipmentInfo
    {
        public string? Brand { get; set; }
        public string? Model { get; set; }
        public string? SerialNumber { get; set; }
        public string? FixedAssetCode { get; set; }
        public string? FenixCode { get; set; }
        public DateTime? AcquisitionDate { get; set; }
    }

    private sealed class TechnicalInfo
    {
        public string? Voltage { get; set; }
        public string? LoadCapacity { get; set; }
        public string? Provider { get; set; }
        public bool RequiresMaintenance { get; set; }
        public bool RequiresPreOperationalCheck { get; set; }
        public bool RequiresCertification { get; set; }
        public DateTime? CertificationExpirationDate { get; set; }
    }

    private sealed class WarrantyInfo
    {
        public bool HasWarranty { get; set; }
        public string? WarrantyType { get; set; }
    }

    private sealed class UsefulLifeInfo
    {
        public DateTime? StartDate { get; set; }
        public int? UsefulLifeMonths { get; set; }
        public int? UsefulLifeDays { get; set; }
    }

    private sealed class MaintenancePlanInfo
    {
        public DateTime? LastMaintenanceDate { get; set; }
        public DateTime? NextMaintenanceDate { get; set; }
        public int? MaintenancePeriodMonths { get; set; }
    }
}

@page "/tools/{ToolId:guid}/accessories"
@rendermode InteractiveServer
@using System.Net.Http.Json
@inject IHttpClientFactory HttpClientFactory
@inject NavigationManager NavigationManager

<PageTitle>Accesorios - NAVI Herramientas</PageTitle>

<div class="page-header">
    <div>
        <button class="btn btn-outline-secondary btn-sm mb-2" @onclick="GoBack">
            ? Volver a hoja de vida
        </button>

        <h1>Gestión de accesorios</h1>
        <p>Agrega, edita o desactiva accesorios asociados a la herramienta.</p>
    </div>

    <button class="btn btn-outline-primary" @onclick="LoadAsync" disabled="@isLoading">
        @(isLoading ? "Cargando..." : "Recargar")
    </button>
</div>

@if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(errorMessage))
{
    <div class="alert alert-danger">
        <strong>Error:</strong> @errorMessage

}

@if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(successMessage))
{
    <div class="alert alert-success">
        @successMessage

}

@code {
    [Parameter]
    public Guid ToolId { get; set; }

    private bool isLoading;
    private bool isSaving;
    private string? errorMessage;
    private string? successMessage;
    private string internalCode = string.Empty;
    private string toolName = string.Empty;
    private Guid? editingAccessoryId;

    private AccessoryFormModel formModel = new();
    private List<AccessoryItemModel> accessories = new();

    protected override async Task OnInitializedAsync()
    {
        await LoadAsync();
    }

    private async Task LoadAsync()
    {
        try
        {
            isLoading = true;
            errorMessage = null;

            var client = HttpClientFactory.CreateClient("NaviApi");

            var record = await client.GetFromJsonAsync<TechnicalLifeRecordHeaderModel>($"api/tools/{ToolId}/technical-life-record");

            if (record is not null)
            {
                internalCode = record.Summary.InternalCode;
                toolName = record.Summary.Name;
            }

            accessories = await client.GetFromJsonAsync<List<AccessoryItemModel>>($"api/tools/{ToolId}/accessories") ?? new();
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            errorMessage = $"No se pudieron cargar los accesorios. Valida que la API esté activa. Detalle: {ex.Message}";
        }
        finally
        {
            isLoading = false;
        }
    }

    private async Task SaveAsync()
    {
        try
        {
            isSaving = true;
            errorMessage = null;
            successMessage = null;

            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(formModel.Name))
            {
                errorMessage = "El nombre del accesorio es obligatorio.";
                return;
            }

            var client = HttpClientFactory.CreateClient("NaviApi");

            HttpResponseMessage response;

            if (editingAccessoryId.HasValue)
            {
                var payload = new
                {
                    name = formModel.Name,
                    quantity = formModel.Quantity <= 0 ? 1 : formModel.Quantity,
                    requiresMaintenance = formModel.RequiresMaintenance,
                    isMeasurementEquipment = formModel.IsMeasurementEquipment,
                    observation = formModel.Observation,
                    updatedBy = "yquinto"
                };

                response = await client.PutAsJsonAsync($"api/tools/accessories/{editingAccessoryId.Value}", payload);
            }
            else
            {
                var payload = new
                {
                    name = formModel.Name,
                    quantity = formModel.Quantity <= 0 ? 1 : formModel.Quantity,
                    requiresMaintenance = formModel.RequiresMaintenance,
                    isMeasurementEquipment = formModel.IsMeasurementEquipment,
                    observation = formModel.Observation,
                    createdBy = "yquinto"
                };

                response = await client.PostAsJsonAsync($"api/tools/{ToolId}/accessories", payload);
            }

            if (!response.IsSuccessStatusCode)
            {
                var detail = await response.Content.ReadAsStringAsync();
                errorMessage = $"No se pudo guardar el accesorio. Código: {(int)response.StatusCode}. Detalle: {detail}";
                return;
            }

            successMessage = editingAccessoryId.HasValue
                ? "Accesorio actualizado correctamente."
                : "Accesorio creado correctamente.";

            CancelEdit();
            await LoadAsync();
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            errorMessage = $"No se pudo guardar el accesorio. Detalle: {ex.Message}";
        }
        finally
        {
            isSaving = false;
        }
    }

    private void StartEdit(AccessoryItemModel item)
    {
        editingAccessoryId = item.Id;

        formModel = new AccessoryFormModel
        {
            Name = item.Name,
            Quantity = item.Quantity,
            RequiresMaintenance = item.RequiresMaintenance,
            IsMeasurementEquipment = item.IsMeasurementEquipment,
            Observation = item.Observation
        };

        successMessage = null;
        errorMessage = null;
    }

    private void CancelEdit()
    {
        editingAccessoryId = null;

        formModel = new AccessoryFormModel
        {
            Quantity = 1
        };
    }

    private async Task DeleteAsync(AccessoryItemModel item)
    {
        try
        {
            isSaving = true;
            errorMessage = null;
            successMessage = null;

            var client = HttpClientFactory.CreateClient("NaviApi");

            var response = await client.DeleteAsync($"api/tools/accessories/{item.Id}?deletedBy=yquinto");

            if (!response.IsSuccessStatusCode)
            {
                var detail = await response.Content.ReadAsStringAsync();
                errorMessage = $"No se pudo desactivar el accesorio. Código: {(int)response.StatusCode}. Detalle: {detail}";
                return;
            }

            successMessage = $"Accesorio desactivado correctamente: {item.Name}.";

            if (editingAccessoryId == item.Id)
            {
                CancelEdit();
            }

            await LoadAsync();
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            errorMessage = $"No se pudo desactivar el accesorio. Detalle: {ex.Message}";
        }
        finally
        {
            isSaving = false;
        }
    }

    private void GoBack()
    {
        NavigationManager.NavigateTo($"/tools/{ToolId}/technical-life-record");
    }

    private static string Show(string? value)
    {
        return string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(value) ? "-" : value;
    }

    private static string BoolText(bool value)
    {
        return value ? "Sí" : "No";
    }

    private sealed class AccessoryFormModel
    {
        public string? Name { get; set; }

        public int Quantity { get; set; } = 1;

        public bool RequiresMaintenance { get; set; }

        public bool IsMeasurementEquipment { get; set; }

        public string? Observation { get; set; }
    }

    private sealed class AccessoryItemModel
    {
        public Guid Id { get; set; }

        public Guid ToolAssetId { get; set; }

        public string Name { get; set; } = string.Empty;

        public int Quantity { get; set; }

        public bool RequiresMaintenance { get; set; }

        public bool IsMeasurementEquipment { get; set; }

        public string? Observation { get; set; }
    }

    private sealed class TechnicalLifeRecordHeaderModel
    {
        public SummaryInfo Summary { get; set; } = new();
    }

    private sealed class SummaryInfo
    {
        public string InternalCode { get; set; } = string.Empty;

        public string Name { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    }
}

<PageTitle>Documentos - NAVI Herramientas</PageTitle>

            Extensiones permitidas: PDF, JPG, JPEG, PNG, XLSX, XLS y DOCX. Tamańo máximo: 50 MB.

    <section class="life-record-section">
        <div class="section-title">
            <span>2</span>
            <h2>Documentos registrados</h2>
        </div>

        @if (isLoading)
        {
            <div class="alert alert-info mb-0">Cargando documentos...</div>
        }
        else if (documents.Count == 0)
        {
            <p class="text-muted mb-0">No hay documentos registrados para esta herramienta.</p>
        }
        else
        {
            <div class="document-card-list">
                @foreach (var item in documents)
                {
                    <div class="document-admin-card">
                        <div class="document-icon">

                                   href="@BuildDownloadUrl(item.DownloadUrl)"
                                   target="_blank">

@code {
    [Parameter]
    public Guid ToolId { get; set; }

    private const long MaxFileSize = 50 * 1024 * 1024;

    private bool isLoading;
    private bool isSaving;
    private string? errorMessage;
    private string? successMessage;
    private string internalCode = string.Empty;
    private string toolName = string.Empty;
    private string apiBaseUrl = string.Empty;

    private IBrowserFile? selectedFile;

    private DocumentUploadFormModel formModel = new()
    {
        DocumentType = "TechnicalDocument"
    };

    private List<DocumentItemModel> documents = new();

    protected override async Task OnInitializedAsync()
    {
        await LoadAsync();
    }

    private async Task LoadAsync()
    {
        try
        {
            isLoading = true;
            errorMessage = null;

            var client = HttpClientFactory.CreateClient("NaviApi");
            apiBaseUrl = client.BaseAddress?.ToString().TrimEnd('/') ?? "http://localhost:5218";

            var record = await client.GetFromJsonAsync<TechnicalLifeRecordHeaderModel>($"api/tools/{ToolId}/technical-life-record");

            if (record is not null)
            {
                internalCode = record.Summary.InternalCode;
                toolName = record.Summary.Name;
            }

            documents = await client.GetFromJsonAsync<List<DocumentItemModel>>($"api/tools/{ToolId}/documents") ?? new();
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            errorMessage = $"No se pudieron cargar los documentos. Valida que la API esté activa. Detalle: {ex.Message}";
        }
        finally
        {
            isLoading = false;
        }
    }

    private void OnFileSelected(InputFileChangeEventArgs e)
    {
        selectedFile = e.File;
        successMessage = null;
        errorMessage = null;
    }

    private async Task UploadAsync()
    {
        if (selectedFile is null)
        {
            errorMessage = "Debe seleccionar un archivo.";
            return;
        }

        try
        {
            isSaving = true;
            errorMessage = null;
            successMessage = null;

            var extension = Path.GetExtension(selectedFile.Name).ToLowerInvariant();
            var allowedExtensions = new[] { ".pdf", ".jpg", ".jpeg", ".png", ".xlsx", ".xls", ".docx" };

            if (!allowedExtensions.Contains(extension))
            {
                errorMessage = "Tipo de archivo no permitido. Use PDF, JPG, JPEG, PNG, XLSX, XLS o DOCX.";
                return;
            }

            if (selectedFile.Size > MaxFileSize)
            {
                errorMessage = "El archivo supera el tamańo máximo permitido de 50 MB.";
                return;
            }

            var client = HttpClientFactory.CreateClient("NaviApi");

            using var form = new MultipartFormDataContent();

            await using var fileStream = selectedFile.OpenReadStream(MaxFileSize);
            using var fileContent = new StreamContent(fileStream);

            fileContent.Headers.ContentType = new MediaTypeHeaderValue(
                string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(selectedFile.ContentType)
                    ? "application/octet-stream"
                    : selectedFile.ContentType);

            form.Add(fileContent, "file", selectedFile.Name);
            form.Add(new StringContent(formModel.DocumentType ?? "Other"), "documentType");
            form.Add(new StringContent(formModel.Description ?? string.Empty), "description");
            form.Add(new StringContent("yquinto"), "uploadedBy");

            var response = await client.PostAsync($"api/tools/{ToolId}/documents", form);

            if (!response.IsSuccessStatusCode)
            {
                var detail = await response.Content.ReadAsStringAsync();
                errorMessage = $"No se pudo cargar el documento. Código: {(int)response.StatusCode}. Detalle: {detail}";
                return;
            }

            successMessage = "Documento cargado correctamente.";

            selectedFile = null;
            formModel = new DocumentUploadFormModel
            {
                DocumentType = "TechnicalDocument"
            };

            await LoadAsync();
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            errorMessage = $"No se pudo cargar el documento. Detalle: {ex.Message}";
        }
        finally
        {
            isSaving = false;
        }
    }

    private async Task DeleteAsync(DocumentItemModel item)
    {
        try
        {
            isSaving = true;
            errorMessage = null;
            successMessage = null;

            var client = HttpClientFactory.CreateClient("NaviApi");

            var response = await client.DeleteAsync($"api/tools/documents/{item.Id}?deletedBy=yquinto");

            if (!response.IsSuccessStatusCode)
            {
                var detail = await response.Content.ReadAsStringAsync();
                errorMessage = $"No se pudo desactivar el documento. Código: {(int)response.StatusCode}. Detalle: {detail}";
                return;
            }

            successMessage = $"Documento desactivado correctamente: {item.FileName}.";
            await LoadAsync();
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            errorMessage = $"No se pudo desactivar el documento. Detalle: {ex.Message}";
        }
        finally
        {
            isSaving = false;
        }
    }

    private void GoBack()
    {
        NavigationManager.NavigateTo($"/tools/{ToolId}/technical-life-record");
    }

    private string BuildDownloadUrl(string? downloadUrl)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(downloadUrl))
        {
            return "#";
        }

        if (downloadUrl.StartsWith("http", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
        {
            return downloadUrl;
        }

        return $"{apiBaseUrl}{downloadUrl}";
    }

    private static string TranslateDocumentType(string? value)
    {
        return value switch
        {
            "TechnicalDocument" => "Documento técnico",
            "PhotographicRecord" => "Registro fotográfico",
            "MaintenanceEvidence" => "Evidencia mantenimiento",
            "Other" => "Otro",
            _ => value ?? "-"
        };
    }

    private static string GetDocumentIcon(string? value)
    {
        return value switch
        {
            "PhotographicRecord" => "???",
            "MaintenanceEvidence" => "??",
            "TechnicalDocument" => "??",
            _ => "??"
        };
    }

    private static string Show(string? value)
    {
        return string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(value) ? "-" : value;
    }

    private static string FormatDate(DateTime value)
    {
        return value.ToString("dd/MM/yyyy HH:mm");
    }

    private static string FormatBytes(long value)
    {
        if (value >= 1024 * 1024)
        {
            return $"{value / 1024d / 1024d:0.00} MB";
        }

        if (value >= 1024)
        {
            return $"{value / 1024d:0.00} KB";
        }

        return $"{value} bytes";
    }

    private sealed class DocumentUploadFormModel
    {
        public string? DocumentType { get; set; }

        public string? Description { get; set; }
    }

    private sealed class DocumentItemModel
    {
        public Guid Id { get; set; }

        public Guid ToolAssetId { get; set; }

        public string DocumentType { get; set; } = string.Empty;

        public string FileName { get; set; } = string.Empty;

        public string? ObjectKey { get; set; }

        public string? ContentType { get; set; }

        public long SizeBytes { get; set; }

        public string? UploadedBy { get; set; }

        public DateTime UploadedAt { get; set; }

        public string? Description { get; set; }

        public string? DownloadUrl { get; set; }
    }

    private sealed class TechnicalLifeRecordHeaderModel
    {
        public SummaryInfo Summary { get; set; } = new();
    }

    private sealed class SummaryInfo
    {
        public string InternalCode { get; set; } = string.Empty;

        public string Name { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    }
}

        {

                {
                    <div class="maintenance-card">
                        <div class="maintenance-card-header">

                        </div>

@code {
    [Parameter]
    public Guid ToolId { get; set; }

    private bool isLoading;
    private bool isSaving;
    private string? errorMessage;
    private string? successMessage;
    private string internalCode = string.Empty;
    private string toolName = string.Empty;
    private Guid? editingMaintenanceId;

    private MaintenanceFormModel formModel = new()
    {
        Type = "Preventive",
        Status = "Scheduled",
        ScheduledAt = DateTime.Today.AddDays(30),
        IsToolOperational = true
    };

    private List<MaintenanceItemModel> maintenanceRecords = new();
    private List<DocumentItemModel> documents = new();

    protected override async Task OnInitializedAsync()
    {
        await LoadAsync();
    }

    private async Task LoadAsync()
    {
        try
        {
            isLoading = true;
            errorMessage = null;

            var client = HttpClientFactory.CreateClient("NaviApi");

            var record = await client.GetFromJsonAsync<TechnicalLifeRecordHeaderModel>($"api/tools/{ToolId}/technical-life-record");

            if (record is not null)
            {
                internalCode = record.Summary.InternalCode;
                toolName = record.Summary.Name;
            }

            maintenanceRecords = await client.GetFromJsonAsync<List<MaintenanceItemModel>>($"api/tools/{ToolId}/maintenance-schedule") ?? new();
            documents = await client.GetFromJsonAsync<List<DocumentItemModel>>($"api/tools/{ToolId}/documents") ?? new();
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            errorMessage = $"No se pudo cargar el cronograma. Valida que la API esté activa. Detalle: {ex.Message}";
        }
        finally
        {
            isLoading = false;
        }
    }

    private async Task SaveAsync()
    {
        try
        {
            isSaving = true;
            errorMessage = null;
            successMessage = null;

            var client = HttpClientFactory.CreateClient("NaviApi");

            HttpResponseMessage response;

            if (editingMaintenanceId.HasValue)
            {
                var payload = BuildPayload("updated");
                response = await client.PutAsJsonAsync($"api/tools/maintenance-schedule/{editingMaintenanceId.Value}", payload);
            }
            else
            {
                var payload = BuildPayload("created");
                response = await client.PostAsJsonAsync($"api/tools/{ToolId}/maintenance-schedule", payload);
            }

            if (!response.IsSuccessStatusCode)
            {
                var detail = await response.Content.ReadAsStringAsync();
                errorMessage = $"No se pudo guardar el mantenimiento. Código: {(int)response.StatusCode}. Detalle: {detail}";
                return;
            }

            successMessage = editingMaintenanceId.HasValue
                ? "Mantenimiento actualizado correctamente."
                : "Mantenimiento creado correctamente.";

            CancelEdit();
            await LoadAsync();
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            errorMessage = $"No se pudo guardar el mantenimiento. Detalle: {ex.Message}";
        }
        finally
        {
            isSaving = false;
        }
    }

    private object BuildPayload(string mode)
    {
        return new
        {
            maintenanceNumber = string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(formModel.MaintenanceNumber)
                ? null
                : formModel.MaintenanceNumber,

            type = formModel.Type,
            status = formModel.Status,
            scheduledAt = formModel.ScheduledAt,
            startedAt = formModel.StartedAt,
            finishedAt = formModel.FinishedAt,
            provider = formModel.Provider,
            technician = formModel.Technician,
            description = formModel.Description,
            maintenanceActivities = formModel.MaintenanceActivities,
            executionNotes = formModel.ExecutionNotes,
            invoiceNumber = formModel.InvoiceNumber,
            responsibleName = formModel.ResponsibleName,
            responsiblePosition = formModel.ResponsiblePosition,
            isToolOperational = formModel.IsToolOperational,
            evidenceDocumentId = GetSelectedEvidenceDocumentId(),
            cost = formModel.Cost,
            result = formModel.Result,
            createdBy = mode == "created" ? "yquinto" : null,
            updatedBy = mode == "updated" ? "yquinto" : null
        };
    }

    private void StartEdit(MaintenanceItemModel item)
    {
        editingMaintenanceId = item.Id;

        formModel = new MaintenanceFormModel
        {
            MaintenanceNumber = item.MaintenanceNumber,
            Type = item.Type,
            Status = item.Status,
            ScheduledAt = item.ScheduledAt.Date,
            StartedAt = item.StartedAt?.Date,
            FinishedAt = item.FinishedAt?.Date,
            Provider = item.Provider,
            Technician = item.Technician,
            Description = item.Description,
            MaintenanceActivities = item.MaintenanceActivities,
            ExecutionNotes = item.ExecutionNotes,
            InvoiceNumber = item.InvoiceNumber,
            ResponsibleName = item.ResponsibleName,
            ResponsiblePosition = item.ResponsiblePosition,
            IsToolOperational = item.IsToolOperational ?? true,
            EvidenceDocumentIdText = item.EvidenceDocumentId?.ToString(),
            Cost = item.Cost,
            Result = item.Result
        };

        successMessage = null;
        errorMessage = null;
    }

    private void CancelEdit()
    {
        editingMaintenanceId = null;

        formModel = new MaintenanceFormModel
        {
            Type = "Preventive",
            Status = "Scheduled",
            ScheduledAt = DateTime.Today.AddDays(30),
            IsToolOperational = true
        };
    }

    private async Task DeleteAsync(MaintenanceItemModel item)
    {
        try
        {
            isSaving = true;
            errorMessage = null;
            successMessage = null;

            var client = HttpClientFactory.CreateClient("NaviApi");

            var response = await client.DeleteAsync($"api/tools/maintenance-schedule/{item.Id}?deletedBy=yquinto");

            if (!response.IsSuccessStatusCode)
            {
                var detail = await response.Content.ReadAsStringAsync();
                errorMessage = $"No se pudo desactivar el mantenimiento. Código: {(int)response.StatusCode}. Detalle: {detail}";
                return;
            }

            successMessage = $"Mantenimiento desactivado correctamente: {item.MaintenanceNumber}.";

            if (editingMaintenanceId == item.Id)
            {
                CancelEdit();
            }

            await LoadAsync();
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            errorMessage = $"No se pudo desactivar el mantenimiento. Detalle: {ex.Message}";
        }
        finally
        {
            isSaving = false;
        }
    }

    private void GoBack()
    {
        NavigationManager.NavigateTo($"/tools/{ToolId}/technical-life-record");
    }

    private string GetSaveButtonText()
    {
        if (isSaving)
        {
            return "Guardando...";
        }

        return editingMaintenanceId.HasValue
            ? "Actualizar mantenimiento"
            : "Crear mantenimiento";
    }

    private static string Show(string? value)
    {
        return string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(value) ? "-" : value;
    }

    private static string FormatDate(DateTime value)
    {
        return value.ToString("dd/MM/yyyy");
    }

    private static string FormatMoney(decimal? value)
    {
        return value.HasValue ? value.Value.ToString("C0") : "-";
    }

    private Guid? GetSelectedEvidenceDocumentId()
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(formModel.EvidenceDocumentIdText))
        {
            return null;
        }

        return Guid.TryParse(formModel.EvidenceDocumentIdText, out var documentId)
            ? documentId
            : null;
    }

    private string GetEvidenceFileName(Guid? documentId)
    {
        if (!documentId.HasValue)
        {
            return "-";
        }

        var document = documents.FirstOrDefault(x => x.Id == documentId.Value);

        return document is null
            ? "-"
            : document.FileName;
    }

    private string GetEvidenceDisplay(Guid? documentId)
    {
        var fileName = GetEvidenceFileName(documentId);

        return fileName == "-"
            ? "-"
            : fileName;
    }

    private bool HasEvidence(Guid? documentId)
    {
        return documentId.HasValue && documents.Any(x => x.Id == documentId.Value);
    }

    private string BuildEvidenceDownloadUrl(Guid? documentId)
    {
        if (!documentId.HasValue)
        {
            return "#";
        }

        var client = HttpClientFactory.CreateClient("NaviApi");
        var baseUrl = client.BaseAddress?.ToString().TrimEnd('/') ?? "http://localhost:5218";

        return $"{baseUrl}/api/tools/documents/{documentId.Value}/download";
    }

    private static string TranslateDocumentType(string? value)
    {
        return value switch
        {
            "TechnicalDocument" => "Documento técnico",
            "PhotographicRecord" => "Registro fotográfico",
            "MaintenanceEvidence" => "Evidencia mantenimiento",
            "Other" => "Otro",
            _ => value ?? "-"
        };
    }

    private static string TranslateType(string? value)
    {
        return value switch
        {
            "Preventive" => "Preventivo",
            "Corrective" => "Correctivo",
            "Calibration" => "Calibración",
            "Inspection" => "Inspección",
            _ => value ?? "-"
        };
    }

    private static string TranslateStatus(string? value)
    {
        return value switch
        {
            "Scheduled" => "Programado",
            "InProgress" => "En proceso",
            "Completed" => "Completado",
            "Cancelled" => "Cancelado",
            _ => value ?? "-"
        };
    }

    private sealed class MaintenanceFormModel
    {
        public string? MaintenanceNumber { get; set; }
        public string Type { get; set; } = "Preventive";
        public string Status { get; set; } = "Scheduled";
        public DateTime ScheduledAt { get; set; }
        public DateTime? StartedAt { get; set; }
        public DateTime? FinishedAt { get; set; }
        public string? Provider { get; set; }
        public string? Technician { get; set; }
        public string? Description { get; set; }
        public string? MaintenanceActivities { get; set; }
        public string? ExecutionNotes { get; set; }
        public string? InvoiceNumber { get; set; }
        public string? ResponsibleName { get; set; }
        public string? ResponsiblePosition { get; set; }
        public bool IsToolOperational { get; set; } = true;
                public string? EvidenceDocumentIdText { get; set; }
        public decimal? Cost { get; set; }
        public string? Result { get; set; }
    }

    private sealed class MaintenanceItemModel
    {
        public Guid Id { get; set; }
        public Guid ToolAssetId { get; set; }
        public string MaintenanceNumber { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string Type { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string Status { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public DateTime ScheduledAt { get; set; }
        public DateTime? StartedAt { get; set; }
        public DateTime? FinishedAt { get; set; }
        public string? Provider { get; set; }
        public string? Technician { get; set; }
        public string? Description { get; set; }
        public string? MaintenanceActivities { get; set; }
        public string? ExecutionNotes { get; set; }
        public string? InvoiceNumber { get; set; }
        public string? ResponsibleName { get; set; }
        public string? ResponsiblePosition { get; set; }
        public bool? IsToolOperational { get; set; }
        public Guid? EvidenceDocumentId { get; set; }
        public decimal? Cost { get; set; }
        public string? Result { get; set; }
    }

    private sealed class DocumentItemModel
    {
        public Guid Id { get; set; }

        public string DocumentType { get; set; } = string.Empty;

        public string FileName { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    }

    private sealed class TechnicalLifeRecordHeaderModel
    {
        public SummaryInfo Summary { get; set; } = new();
    }

    private sealed class SummaryInfo
    {
        public string InternalCode { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string Name { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    }
}

        @if (isLoading)

                            <p>@item.Description</p>

                            <div class="d-flex gap-1 flex-wrap mt-2">
                                <button class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-primary" @onclick="() => StartEdit(item)">
                                    Editar
                                </button>

                                <button class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-danger" @onclick="() => DeleteAsync(item)">
                                    Desactivar
                                </button>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                }
            </div>
        }
    </section>
</div>

@code {
    [Parameter]
    public Guid ToolId { get; set; }

    private bool isLoading;
    private bool isSaving;
    private string? errorMessage;
    private string? successMessage;
    private string internalCode = string.Empty;
    private string toolName = string.Empty;
    private Guid? editingSafePracticeId;

    private SafePracticeFormModel formModel = new()
    {
        SortOrder = 1
    };

    private List<SafePracticeItemModel> safePractices = new();

    protected override async Task OnInitializedAsync()
    {
        await LoadAsync();
    }

    private async Task LoadAsync()
    {
        try
        {
            isLoading = true;
            errorMessage = null;

            var client = HttpClientFactory.CreateClient("NaviApi");

            var record = await client.GetFromJsonAsync<TechnicalLifeRecordHeaderModel>($"api/tools/{ToolId}/technical-life-record");

            if (record is not null)
            {
                internalCode = record.Summary.InternalCode;
                toolName = record.Summary.Name;
            }

            safePractices = await client.GetFromJsonAsync<List<SafePracticeItemModel>>($"api/tools/{ToolId}/safe-practices") ?? new();

            if (!editingSafePracticeId.HasValue && safePractices.Count > 0 && formModel.SortOrder <= 1)
            {
                formModel.SortOrder = safePractices.Max(x => x.SortOrder) + 1;
            }
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            errorMessage = $"No se pudieron cargar las prácticas seguras. Valida que la API esté activa. Detalle: {ex.Message}";
        }
        finally
        {
            isLoading = false;
        }
    }

    private async Task SaveAsync()
    {
        try
        {
            isSaving = true;
            errorMessage = null;
            successMessage = null;

            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(formModel.PracticeName))
            {
                errorMessage = "El nombre de la práctica segura es obligatorio.";
                return;
            }

            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(formModel.Description))
            {
                errorMessage = "La descripción de la práctica segura es obligatoria.";
                return;
            }

            var client = HttpClientFactory.CreateClient("NaviApi");

            HttpResponseMessage response;

            if (editingSafePracticeId.HasValue)
            {
                var payload = new
                {
                    practiceName = formModel.PracticeName,
                    description = formModel.Description,
                    sortOrder = formModel.SortOrder,
                    updatedBy = "yquinto"
                };

                response = await client.PutAsJsonAsync($"api/tools/safe-practices/{editingSafePracticeId.Value}", payload);
            }
            else
            {
                var payload = new
                {
                    practiceName = formModel.PracticeName,
                    description = formModel.Description,
                    sortOrder = formModel.SortOrder,
                    createdBy = "yquinto"
                };

                response = await client.PostAsJsonAsync($"api/tools/{ToolId}/safe-practices", payload);
            }

            if (!response.IsSuccessStatusCode)
            {
                var detail = await response.Content.ReadAsStringAsync();
                errorMessage = $"No se pudo guardar la práctica segura. Código: {(int)response.StatusCode}. Detalle: {detail}";
                return;
            }

            successMessage = editingSafePracticeId.HasValue
                ? "Práctica segura actualizada correctamente."
                : "Práctica segura creada correctamente.";

            CancelEdit();
            await LoadAsync();
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            errorMessage = $"No se pudo guardar la práctica segura. Detalle: {ex.Message}";
        }
        finally
        {
            isSaving = false;
        }
    }

    private async Task CreateDefaultsAsync()
    {
        try
        {
            isSaving = true;
            errorMessage = null;
            successMessage = null;

            var client = HttpClientFactory.CreateClient("NaviApi");

            var response = await client.PostAsync($"api/tools/{ToolId}/safe-practices/defaults", null);

            if (!response.IsSuccessStatusCode)
            {
                var detail = await response.Content.ReadAsStringAsync();
                errorMessage = $"No se pudieron cargar prácticas predeterminadas. Código: {(int)response.StatusCode}. Detalle: {detail}";
                return;
            }

            successMessage = "Prácticas seguras predeterminadas cargadas correctamente.";
            await LoadAsync();
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            errorMessage = $"No se pudieron cargar prácticas predeterminadas. Detalle: {ex.Message}";
        }
        finally
        {
            isSaving = false;
        }
    }

    private void StartEdit(SafePracticeItemModel item)
    {
        editingSafePracticeId = item.Id;

        formModel = new SafePracticeFormModel
        {
            PracticeName = item.PracticeName,
            Description = item.Description,
            SortOrder = item.SortOrder
        };

        successMessage = null;
        errorMessage = null;
    }

    private void CancelEdit()
    {
        editingSafePracticeId = null;

        var nextOrder = safePractices.Count == 0
            ? 1
            : safePractices.Max(x => x.SortOrder) + 1;

        formModel = new SafePracticeFormModel
        {
            SortOrder = nextOrder
        };
    }

    private async Task DeleteAsync(SafePracticeItemModel item)
    {
        try
        {
            isSaving = true;
            errorMessage = null;
            successMessage = null;

            var client = HttpClientFactory.CreateClient("NaviApi");

            var response = await client.DeleteAsync($"api/tools/safe-practices/{item.Id}?deletedBy=yquinto");

            if (!response.IsSuccessStatusCode)
            {
                var detail = await response.Content.ReadAsStringAsync();
                errorMessage = $"No se pudo desactivar la práctica segura. Código: {(int)response.StatusCode}. Detalle: {detail}";
                return;
            }

            successMessage = $"Práctica segura desactivada correctamente: {item.PracticeName}.";

            if (editingSafePracticeId == item.Id)
            {
                CancelEdit();
            }

            await LoadAsync();
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            errorMessage = $"No se pudo desactivar la práctica segura. Detalle: {ex.Message}";
        }
        finally
        {
            isSaving = false;
        }
    }

    private void GoBack()
    {
        NavigationManager.NavigateTo($"/tools/{ToolId}/technical-life-record");
    }

    private string GetSaveButtonText()
    {
        if (isSaving)
        {
            return "Guardando...";
        }

        return editingSafePracticeId.HasValue
            ? "Actualizar práctica"
            : "Crear práctica";
    }

    private sealed class SafePracticeFormModel
    {
        public string? PracticeName { get; set; }

        public string? Description { get; set; }

        public int SortOrder { get; set; }
    }

    private sealed class SafePracticeItemModel
    {
        public Guid Id { get; set; }

        public Guid ToolAssetId { get; set; }

        public string PracticeName { get; set; } = string.Empty;

        public string Description { get; set; } = string.Empty;

        public int SortOrder { get; set; }
    }

    private sealed class TechnicalLifeRecordHeaderModel
    {
        public SummaryInfo Summary { get; set; } = new();
    }

    private sealed class SummaryInfo
    {
        public string InternalCode { get; set; } = string.Empty;

        public string Name { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    }
}

@using System.Net.Http.Json

<PageTitle>Trazabilidad de hoja de vida</PageTitle>

<div class="page-header">

        <a class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-secondary" href="@($"/tools/{ToolId}/technical-life-record")">

        <h1>Trazabilidad de hoja de vida</h1>

    </div>

    <button class="btn btn-primary" @onclick="LoadAsync">
        Recargar
    </button>
</div>

@if (isLoading)
{
    <p>Cargando trazabilidad...</p>
}
else if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(errorMessage))
{
    <div class="alert alert-danger">@errorMessage</div>
}
else if (record is null)
{
    <div class="alert alert-warning">No se encontró información de la herramienta.</div>
}

{
    <section class="life-record-cover">

            <span class="cover-tag">Trazabilidad</span>

                   value="@searchText"

                   placeholder="Ej: documento, mantenimiento, evidencia, accesorio..." />

                Limpiar filtros
            </button>

    </section>

    

    @if (filteredEvents.Count == 0)
    {

        </div>
    }
    else
    {

            @foreach (var item in filteredEvents)

                        <span>@FormatTime(item.EventDate)</span>
                    </div>

                    <div class="traceability-content">
                        <div class="traceability-header">
                            <span class="traceability-type">@TranslateEventType(item.EventType)</span>
                            <strong>@Show(item.Title)</strong>
                        </div>

@code {
    [Parameter]
    public Guid ToolId { get; set; }

    private TechnicalLifeRecordModel? record;
    private bool isLoading = true;
    private string? errorMessage;
    private string searchText = string.Empty;
    private string selectedEventType = string.Empty;
    private List<LifeCycleEventModel> filteredEvents = new();

    private IEnumerable<string> EventTypes =>
        record?.LifeCycleEvents
            .Select(x => x.EventType)
            .Where(x => !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(x))
            .Distinct(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .OrderBy(x => TranslateEventType(x))
        ?? Enumerable.Empty<string>();

    private IEnumerable<EventTypeOption> EventTypeOptions =>
        record?.LifeCycleEvents
            .Where(x => !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(x.EventType))
            .GroupBy(x => x.EventType.Trim(), StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .Select(x => new EventTypeOption
            {
                Value = x.Key,
                Label = TranslateEventType(x.Key),
                Count = x.Count()
            })
            .OrderBy(x => x.Label)
        ?? Enumerable.Empty<EventTypeOption>();

    protected override async Task OnInitializedAsync()
    {
        await LoadAsync();
    }

    private async Task LoadAsync()
    {
        try
        {
            isLoading = true;
            errorMessage = null;

            var client = HttpClientFactory.CreateClient("NaviApi");

            record = await client.GetFromJsonAsync<TechnicalLifeRecordModel>(
                $"api/tools/{ToolId}/technical-life-record");

            ApplyFilters();
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            errorMessage = $"No se pudo cargar la trazabilidad. Detalle: {ex.Message}";
        }
        finally
        {
            isLoading = false;
        }
    }

    private void OnSearchTextChanged(ChangeEventArgs args)
    {
        searchText = args.Value?.ToString() ?? string.Empty;
        ApplyFilters();
    }

    private void OnEventTypeChanged(ChangeEventArgs args)
    {
        selectedEventType = args.Value?.ToString() ?? string.Empty;
        ApplyFilters();
    }

    private void SelectEventType(string value)
    {
        selectedEventType = value;
        ApplyFilters();
    }

    private void ApplyFilters()
    {
        var query = record?.LifeCycleEvents.AsEnumerable()
            ?? Enumerable.Empty<LifeCycleEventModel>();

        var eventTypeFilter = selectedEventType?.Trim() ?? string.Empty;
        var textFilter = searchText?.Trim() ?? string.Empty;

        if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(eventTypeFilter))
        {
            query = query.Where(x =>
                string.Equals(x.EventType?.Trim(), eventTypeFilter, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase));
        }

        if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(textFilter))
        {
            query = query.Where(x =>
                Contains(x.EventType, textFilter) ||
                Contains(TranslateEventType(x.EventType), textFilter) ||
                Contains(x.Title, textFilter) ||
                Contains(x.Description, textFilter) ||
                Contains(x.PreviousValue, textFilter) ||
                Contains(x.NewValue, textFilter) ||
                Contains(x.PerformedBy, textFilter));
        }

        filteredEvents = query
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.EventDate)
            .ToList();

        StateHasChanged();
    }

    private void ClearFilters()
    {
        searchText = string.Empty;
        selectedEventType = string.Empty;
        ApplyFilters();
    }

    private string GetFilterButtonClass(string value)
    {
        var isActive = string.Equals(
            selectedEventType?.Trim() ?? string.Empty,
            value?.Trim() ?? string.Empty,
            StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        return isActive
            ? "traceability-filter-chip active"
            : "traceability-filter-chip";
    }

    private static string TranslateEventType(string? value)
    {
        return value switch
        {
            "DefaultSafePracticesCreated" => "Prácticas seguras creadas",
            "DocumentDeleted" => "Documento eliminado",
            "DocumentUploaded" => "Documento cargado",
            "MaintenanceEvidenceDocumentCleared" => "Evidencia limpiada",
            "MaintenanceScheduleCreated" => "Mantenimiento creado",
            "MaintenanceScheduleDeleted" => "Mantenimiento eliminado",
            "MaintenanceScheduleUpdated" => "Mantenimiento actualizado",
            "MockTechnicalLifeRecordDataApplied" => "Datos simulados aplicados",
            "TechnicalDataUpdated" => "Datos técnicos actualizados",
            "ToolAccessoryCreated" => "Accesorio creado",
            "ToolAccessoryUpdated" => "Accesorio actualizado",
            "ToolAccessoryDeleted" => "Accesorio eliminado",
            "DefaultSafePracticesApplied" => "Prácticas aplicadas",
            "ToolSafePracticeCreated" => "Práctica segura creada",
            "ToolSafePracticeUpdated" => "Práctica segura actualizada",
            "ToolSafePracticeDeleted" => "Práctica segura eliminada",
            _ => string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(value) ? "Sin tipo" : value
        };
    }

    private static bool Contains(string? value, string filter)
    {
        return !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(value)
            && value.Contains(filter, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
    }

    private static string Show(string? value)
    {
        return string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(value) ? "-" : value;
    }

    private static string FormatDate(DateTime value)
    {
        return value.ToString("dd/MM/yyyy");
    }

    private static string FormatTime(DateTime value)
    {
        return value.ToString("HH:mm");
    }

    private sealed class EventTypeOption
    {
        public string Value { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string Label { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public int Count { get; set; }
    }

    private sealed class TechnicalLifeRecordModel
    {
        public SummaryModel Summary { get; set; } = new();
        public List<LifeCycleEventModel> LifeCycleEvents { get; set; } = new();
    }

    private sealed class SummaryModel
    {
        public string InternalCode { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string Name { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    }

    private sealed class LifeCycleEventModel
    {
        public Guid Id { get; set; }
        public string EventType { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string Title { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string? Description { get; set; }
        public string? PreviousValue { get; set; }
        public string? NewValue { get; set; }
        public string? PerformedBy { get; set; }
        public DateTime EventDate { get; set; }
    }
}

FILE: C:\Users\yquinto\OneDrive - Navitrans\Escritorio\Documentos\Herramientas\Herramientas&Activos\src\Navi.ToolsAssets.Admin\Components\Pages\Modules\CatalogsSettings.razor

@page "/settings/catalogs"

<PageTitle>Tipos y categorías</PageTitle>

@page "/settings/branches"
@rendermode InteractiveServer
@inject IHttpClientFactory HttpClientFactory

<PageTitle>Sedes - Configuración</PageTitle>

<section class="settings-entity-banner">
    <div>
        <span class="settings-entity-pill">ORGANIZACIÓN</span>
        <h2>Sedes</h2>
        <p>Administra las sedes operativas donde se ubican herramientas, activos, talleres y almacenes.</p>
    </div>

        <div class="settings-entity-status">
            <span>Sedes</span>

        </a>
    </div>
</section>

<section class="settings-crud-layout">
    <div class="settings-crud-form">
        <h2>@(editingId is null ? "Crear sede" : "Editar sede")</h2>

        <EditForm Model="formModel" OnValidSubmit="SaveAsync">
            <DataAnnotationsValidator />

            <div class="mb-3">
                <label class="form-label">Código</label>
                <InputText class="form-control" @bind-Value="formModel.Code" placeholder="AGU, MED, BOG" />
            </div>

            <div class="mb-3">
                <label class="form-label">Nombre</label>
                <InputText class="form-control" @bind-Value="formModel.Name" />
            </div>

            <div class="mb-3">
                <label class="form-label">Ciudad</label>
                <InputText class="form-control" @bind-Value="formModel.City" />
            </div>

            <div class="mb-3">
                <label class="form-label">Dirección</label>
                <InputText class="form-control" @bind-Value="formModel.Address" />
            </div>

            <div class="mb-3">
                <label class="form-label">Zona</label>
                <InputSelect class="form-select" @bind-Value="formModel.ZoneId">
                    <option value="">Seleccione zona</option>
                    @foreach (var zone in zones)
                    {
                        <option value="@zone.Id">@zone.Code - @zone.Name</option>
                    }
                </InputSelect>
            </div>

            <div class="form-check mb-2">
                <InputCheckbox class="form-check-input" @bind-Value="formModel.IsPilot" />
                <label class="form-check-label">Sede piloto</label>
            </div>

            <div class="form-check mb-3">
                <InputCheckbox class="form-check-input" @bind-Value="formModel.IsActive" />
                <label class="form-check-label">Activa</label>
            </div>

            @if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(message))
            {
                <div class="@messageClass">@message</div>
            }

            <div class="settings-crud-actions">
                <button class="btn btn-primary" type="submit">Guardar</button>
                <button class="btn btn-outline-secondary" type="button" @onclick="ClearForm">Limpiar</button>
            </div>
        </EditForm>
    </div>

    <div class="settings-crud-table">
        <div class="settings-table-header">
            <h2>Sedes registradas</h2>
            <button class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-primary" @onclick="LoadAsync">Actualizar</button>
        </div>

        @if (isLoading)
        {
            <p>Cargando sedes...</p>
        }
        else
        {
            <table class="table table-hover align-middle">
                <thead>
                    <tr>
                        <th>Código</th>

                        <th>Ciudad</th>
                        <th>Zona</th>
                        <th>Estado</th>
                        <th class="text-end">Acciones</th>
                    </tr>
                </thead>
                <tbody>
                    @foreach (var branch in branches)
                    {
                        <tr>
                            <td><strong>@branch.Code</strong></td>
                            <td>
                                <div>@branch.Name</div>
                                <small class="text-muted">@branch.Address</small>
                            </td>
                            <td>@branch.City</td>
                            <td>@(branch.Zone is null ? "Sin zona" : $"{branch.Zone.Code} - {branch.Zone.Name}")</td>
                            <td>
                                <span class="badge @(branch.IsActive ? "bg-success" : "bg-secondary")">
                                    @(branch.IsActive ? "Activa" : "Inactiva")
                                </span>
                            </td>
                            <td class="text-end">
                                <button class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-primary" @onclick="() => Edit(branch)">Editar</button>
                                <button class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-danger" @onclick="() => DeleteAsync(branch.Id)">Eliminar</button>
                            </td>
                        </tr>
