@code {
    private HttpClient Api => HttpClientFactory.CreateClient("NaviApi");

    private List<BranchDto> branches = new();
    private List<ZoneDto> zones = new();
    private BranchFormModel formModel = new();
    private Guid? editingId;
    private bool isLoading;
    private string message = string.Empty;
    private string messageClass = "alert alert-info";

    protected override async Task OnInitializedAsync()
    {
        await LoadAsync();
    }

    private async Task LoadAsync()
    {
        isLoading = true;
        message = string.Empty;

        try
        {
            branches = await Api.GetFromJsonAsync<List<BranchDto>>("api/settings/branches") ?? new();
            zones = await Api.GetFromJsonAsync<List<ZoneDto>>("api/settings/zones") ?? new();
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            ShowError($"No se pudieron cargar las sedes: {ex.Message}");
        }
        finally
        {
            isLoading = false;
        }
    }

    private async Task SaveAsync()
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(formModel.Code) ||
            string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(formModel.Name) ||
            formModel.ZoneId is null)
        {
            ShowError("Código, nombre y zona son obligatorios.");
            return;
        }

        var request = new
        {
            code = formModel.Code,
            name = formModel.Name,
            city = formModel.City,
            address = formModel.Address,
            zoneId = formModel.ZoneId.Value,
            isPilot = formModel.IsPilot,
            isActive = formModel.IsActive,
            changedBy = "admin-web"
        };

        try
        {
            HttpResponseMessage response = editingId is null
                ? await Api.PostAsJsonAsync("api/settings/branches", request)
                : await Api.PutAsJsonAsync($"api/settings/branches/{editingId}", request);

            if (!response.IsSuccessStatusCode)
            {
                ShowError(await response.Content.ReadAsStringAsync());
                return;
            }

            ShowSuccess(editingId is null ? "Sede creada correctamente." : "Sede actualizada correctamente.");
            ClearForm();
            await LoadAsync();
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            ShowError($"Error guardando sede: {ex.Message}");
        }
    }

    private void Edit(BranchDto branch)
    {
        editingId = branch.Id;

        formModel = new BranchFormModel
        {
            Code = branch.Code,
            Name = branch.Name,
            City = branch.City,
            Address = branch.Address,
            ZoneId = branch.ZoneId,
            IsPilot = branch.IsPilot,
            IsActive = branch.IsActive
        };
    }

    private async Task DeleteAsync(Guid id)
    {
        try
        {
            var response = await Api.DeleteAsync($"api/settings/branches/{id}?changedBy=admin-web");

            if (!response.IsSuccessStatusCode)
            {
                ShowError(await response.Content.ReadAsStringAsync());
                return;
            }

            ShowSuccess("Sede eliminada correctamente.");
            await LoadAsync();
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            ShowError($"Error eliminando sede: {ex.Message}");
        }
    }

    private void ClearForm()
    {
        editingId = null;
        formModel = new BranchFormModel();
    }

    private void ShowSuccess(string value)
    {
        message = value;
        messageClass = "alert alert-success";
    }

    private void ShowError(string value)
    {
        message = value;
        messageClass = "alert alert-danger";
    }

    private sealed class BranchDto
    {
        public Guid Id { get; set; }
        public string Code { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string Name { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string? City { get; set; }
        public string? Address { get; set; }
        public Guid ZoneId { get; set; }
        public ZoneDto? Zone { get; set; }
        public bool IsPilot { get; set; }
        public bool IsActive { get; set; }
    }

    private sealed class ZoneDto
    {
        public Guid Id { get; set; }
        public string Code { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string Name { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    }

    private sealed class BranchFormModel
    {
        public string Code { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string Name { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string? City { get; set; }
        public string? Address { get; set; }
        public Guid? ZoneId { get; set; }
        public bool IsPilot { get; set; }
        public bool IsActive { get; set; } = true;
    }
}

@page "/settings/locations"
@rendermode InteractiveServer
@inject IHttpClientFactory HttpClientFactory

<PageTitle>Ubicaciones - Configuración</PageTitle>

<section class="settings-entity-banner">
    <div>
        <span class="settings-entity-pill">ORGANIZACIÓN</span>
        <h2>Ubicaciones internas</h2>
        <p>Administra estantes, bahías, zonas internas, puestos técnicos y ubicaciones físicas dentro de sedes, almacenes o talleres.</p>
    </div>

    <div class="settings-entity-side">
        <div class="settings-entity-status">
            <span>Ubicaciones</span>
            <strong>@locations.Count registradas</strong>
        </div>

        <a class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-light settings-entity-back" href="/settings">
            Volver a Configuración
        </a>
    </div>
</section>

<section class="settings-crud-layout">
    <div class="settings-crud-form">
        <h2>@(editingId is null ? "Crear ubicación" : "Editar ubicación")</h2>

        <EditForm Model="formModel" OnValidSubmit="SaveAsync">
            <DataAnnotationsValidator />

            <div class="mb-3">
                <label class="form-label">Código</label>
                <InputText class="form-control" @bind-Value="formModel.Code" placeholder="AGU-EST-A1, AGU-BAHIA-03" />
            </div>

            <div class="mb-3">
                <label class="form-label">Nombre</label>
                <InputText class="form-control" @bind-Value="formModel.Name" placeholder="Estante A1, Bahía 03, Zona eléctrica" />
            </div>

            <div class="mb-3">
                <label class="form-label">Sede</label>
                <InputSelect class="form-select" @bind-Value="formModel.BranchId">
                    <option value="">Seleccione sede</option>
                    @foreach (var branch in branches)
                    {
                        <option value="@branch.Id">@branch.Code - @branch.Name</option>
                    }
                </InputSelect>
            </div>

            <div class="mb-3">
                <label class="form-label">Descripción</label>
                <InputTextArea class="form-control" @bind-Value="formModel.Description" rows="3" placeholder="Ubicación interna dentro de un almacén, taller o zona operativa." />
            </div>

            <div class="form-check mb-3">
                <InputCheckbox class="form-check-input" @bind-Value="formModel.IsActive" />
                <label class="form-check-label">Activa</label>
            </div>

            @if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(message))
            {
                <div class="@messageClass">@message</div>
            }

            <div class="settings-crud-actions">
                <button class="btn btn-primary" type="submit">Guardar</button>
                <button class="btn btn-outline-secondary" type="button" @onclick="ClearForm">Limpiar</button>
            </div>
        </EditForm>
    </div>

    <div class="settings-crud-table">
        <div class="settings-table-header">
            <h2>Ubicaciones registradas</h2>
            <button class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-primary" @onclick="LoadAsync">Actualizar</button>
        </div>

        @if (isLoading)
        {
            <p>Cargando ubicaciones...</p>
        }
        else if (locations.Count == 0)
        {
            <div class="alert alert-info">No hay ubicaciones registradas.</div>
        }
        else
        {
            <table class="table table-hover align-middle">
                <thead>
                    <tr>
                        <th>Código</th>
                        <th>Nombre</th>
                        <th>Sede</th>
                        <th>Descripción</th>
                        <th>Estado</th>
                        <th class="text-end">Acciones</th>
                    </tr>
                </thead>
                <tbody>
                    @foreach (var location in locations)
                    {
                        <tr>
                            <td><strong>@location.Code</strong></td>
                            <td>@location.Name</td>
                            <td>@(location.Branch is null ? "Sin sede" : $"{location.Branch.Code} - {location.Branch.Name}")</td>
                            <td>
                                <span class="settings-description-cell">
                                    @location.Description
                                </span>
                            </td>
                            <td>
                                <span class="badge @(location.IsActive ? "bg-success" : "bg-secondary")">
                                    @(location.IsActive ? "Activa" : "Inactiva")
                                </span>
                            </td>
                            <td class="text-end">
                                <button class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-primary" @onclick="() => Edit(location)">Editar</button>
                                <button class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-danger" @onclick="() => DeleteAsync(location.Id)">Eliminar</button>
                            </td>
                        </tr>
                    }
                </tbody>
            </table>
        }
    </div>
</section>

@code {
    private HttpClient Api => HttpClientFactory.CreateClient("NaviApi");

    private List<LocationDto> locations = new();
    private List<BranchDto> branches = new();
    private LocationFormModel formModel = new();
    private Guid? editingId;
    private bool isLoading;
    private string message = string.Empty;
    private string messageClass = "alert alert-info";

    protected override async Task OnInitializedAsync()
    {
        await LoadAsync();
    }

    private async Task LoadAsync()
    {
        isLoading = true;
        message = string.Empty;

        try
        {
            locations = await Api.GetFromJsonAsync<List<LocationDto>>("api/settings/warehouses") ?? new();
            branches = await Api.GetFromJsonAsync<List<BranchDto>>("api/settings/branches") ?? new();
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            ShowError($"No se pudieron cargar las ubicaciones: {ex.Message}");
        }
        finally
        {
            isLoading = false;
        }
    }

    private async Task SaveAsync()
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(formModel.Code) ||
            string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(formModel.Name) ||
            formModel.BranchId is null)
        {
            ShowError("Código, nombre y sede son obligatorios.");
            return;
        }

        var request = new
        {
            code = formModel.Code,
            name = formModel.Name,
            description = formModel.Description,
            branchId = formModel.BranchId.Value,
            isActive = formModel.IsActive,
            changedBy = "admin-web"
        };

        try
        {
            HttpResponseMessage response = editingId is null
                ? await Api.PostAsJsonAsync("api/settings/warehouses", request)
                : await Api.PutAsJsonAsync($"api/settings/warehouses/{editingId}", request);

            if (!response.IsSuccessStatusCode)
            {
                ShowError(await response.Content.ReadAsStringAsync());
                return;
            }

            ShowSuccess(editingId is null ? "Ubicación creada correctamente." : "Ubicación actualizada correctamente.");
            ClearForm();
            await LoadAsync();
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            ShowError($"Error guardando ubicación: {ex.Message}");
        }
    }

    private void Edit(LocationDto location)
    {
        editingId = location.Id;

        formModel = new LocationFormModel
        {
            Code = location.Code,
            Name = location.Name,
            Description = location.Description,
            BranchId = location.BranchId,
            IsActive = location.IsActive
        };
    }

    private async Task DeleteAsync(Guid id)
    {
        try
        {
            var response = await Api.DeleteAsync($"api/settings/warehouses/{id}?changedBy=admin-web");

            if (!response.IsSuccessStatusCode)
            {
                ShowError(await response.Content.ReadAsStringAsync());
                return;
            }

            ShowSuccess("Ubicación eliminada correctamente.");
            await LoadAsync();
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            ShowError($"Error eliminando ubicación: {ex.Message}");
        }
    }

    private void ClearForm()
    {
        editingId = null;
        formModel = new LocationFormModel();
    }

    private void ShowSuccess(string value)
    {
        message = value;
        messageClass = "alert alert-success";
    }

    private void ShowError(string value)
    {
        message = value;
        messageClass = "alert alert-danger";
    }

    private sealed class LocationDto
    {
        public Guid Id { get; set; }
        public string Code { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string Name { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string? Description { get; set; }
        public Guid BranchId { get; set; }
        public BranchDto? Branch { get; set; }
        public bool IsActive { get; set; }
    }

    private sealed class BranchDto
    {
        public Guid Id { get; set; }
        public string Code { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string Name { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    }

    private sealed class LocationFormModel
    {
        public string Code { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string Name { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string? Description { get; set; }
        public Guid? BranchId { get; set; }
        public bool IsActive { get; set; } = true;
    }
}

            @if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(message))

    <div class="settings-crud-table">
        <div class="settings-table-header">
            <h2>Responsables registrados</h2>
            <button class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-primary" @onclick="LoadAsync">Actualizar</button>
        </div>

        @if (isLoading)
        {
            <p>Cargando responsables...</p>
        }
        else
        {
            <table class="table table-hover align-middle">
                <thead>
                    <tr>
                        <th>Código</th>
                        <th>Nombre</th>
                        <th>Cargo</th>
                        <th>Área</th>
                        <th>Estado</th>
                        <th class="text-end">Acciones</th>
                    </tr>
                </thead>
                <tbody>
                    @foreach (var item in items)
                    {
                        <tr>

                                    @(item.IsActive ? "Activo" : "Inactivo")

@code {
    private HttpClient Api => HttpClientFactory.CreateClient("NaviApi");

    private List<ResponsibleDto> items = new();
    private ResponsibleFormModel formModel = new();
    private Guid? editingId;
    private bool isLoading;
    private string message = string.Empty;
    private string messageClass = "alert alert-info";

    protected override async Task OnInitializedAsync()
    {
        await LoadAsync();
    }

    private async Task LoadAsync()
    {
        isLoading = true;
        message = string.Empty;

        try
        {
            items = await Api.GetFromJsonAsync<List<ResponsibleDto>>("api/settings/responsibles") ?? new();
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            ShowError($"No se pudieron cargar los responsables: {ex.Message}");
        }
        finally
        {
            isLoading = false;
        }
    }

    private async Task SaveAsync()
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(formModel.FullName))
        {
            ShowError("El nombre completo es obligatorio.");
            return;
        }

        var request = new
        {
            employeeCode = formModel.EmployeeCode,
            documentNumber = formModel.DocumentNumber,
            fullName = formModel.FullName,
            email = formModel.Email,
            position = formModel.Position,
            area = formModel.Area,
            isActive = formModel.IsActive,
            changedBy = "admin-web"
        };

        try
        {
            HttpResponseMessage response = editingId is null
                ? await Api.PostAsJsonAsync("api/settings/responsibles", request)
                : await Api.PutAsJsonAsync($"api/settings/responsibles/{editingId}", request);

            if (!response.IsSuccessStatusCode)
            {
                ShowError(await response.Content.ReadAsStringAsync());
                return;
            }

            ShowSuccess(editingId is null ? "Responsable creado correctamente." : "Responsable actualizado correctamente.");
            ClearForm();
            await LoadAsync();
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            ShowError($"Error guardando responsable: {ex.Message}");
        }
    }

    private void Edit(ResponsibleDto item)
    {
        editingId = item.Id;

        formModel = new ResponsibleFormModel
        {
            EmployeeCode = item.EmployeeCode,
            DocumentNumber = item.DocumentNumber,
            FullName = item.FullName,
            Email = item.Email,
            Position = item.Position,
            Area = item.Area,
            IsActive = item.IsActive
        };
    }

    private async Task DeleteAsync(Guid id)
    {
        try
        {
            var response = await Api.DeleteAsync($"api/settings/responsibles/{id}?changedBy=admin-web");

            if (!response.IsSuccessStatusCode)
            {
                ShowError(await response.Content.ReadAsStringAsync());
                return;
            }

            ShowSuccess("Responsable eliminado correctamente.");
            await LoadAsync();
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            ShowError($"Error eliminando responsable: {ex.Message}");
        }
    }

    private void ClearForm()
    {
        editingId = null;
        formModel = new ResponsibleFormModel();
    }

    private void ShowSuccess(string value)
    {
        message = value;
        messageClass = "alert alert-success";
    }

    private void ShowError(string value)
    {
        message = value;
        messageClass = "alert alert-danger";
    }

    private sealed class ResponsibleDto
    {
        public Guid Id { get; set; }
        public string? EmployeeCode { get; set; }
        public string? DocumentNumber { get; set; }
        public string FullName { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string? Email { get; set; }
        public string? Position { get; set; }
        public string? Area { get; set; }
        public bool IsActive { get; set; }
    }

    private sealed class ResponsibleFormModel
    {
        public string? EmployeeCode { get; set; }
        public string? DocumentNumber { get; set; }
        public string FullName { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string? Email { get; set; }
        public string? Position { get; set; }
        public string? Area { get; set; }
        public bool IsActive { get; set; } = true;
    }
}

                new PermissionItem("WAREHOUSES.MANAGE", "Gestionar almacenes"),
                new PermissionItem("CATALOGS.MANAGE", "Gestionar catálogos")
            }
        }
    };

    protected override async Task OnInitializedAsync()
    {
        await LoadAsync();
    }

    private async Task LoadAsync()
    {
        isLoading = true;
        message = string.Empty;

        try
        {
            roles = await Api.GetFromJsonAsync<List<RoleDto>>("api/settings/roles") ?? new();
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            ShowError($"No se pudieron cargar los roles: {ex.Message}");
        }
        finally
        {
            isLoading = false;
        }
    }

    private async Task SaveAsync()
    {
        message = string.Empty;

        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(formModel.Code) || string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(formModel.Name))
        {
            ShowError("Código y nombre son obligatorios.");
            return;
        }

        formModel.Permissions = string.Join(",", selectedPermissions.OrderBy(x => x));

        var request = new
        {
            code = formModel.Code,
            name = formModel.Name,
            description = formModel.Description,
            permissions = formModel.Permissions,
            isActive = formModel.IsActive,
            changedBy = "admin-web"
        };

        try
        {
            HttpResponseMessage response;

            if (editingId is null)
            {
                response = await Api.PostAsJsonAsync("api/settings/roles", request);
            }
            else
            {
                response = await Api.PutAsJsonAsync($"api/settings/roles/{editingId}", request);
            }

            if (!response.IsSuccessStatusCode)
            {
                var error = await response.Content.ReadAsStringAsync();
                ShowError(error);
                return;
            }

            ShowSuccess(editingId is null ? "Rol creado correctamente." : "Rol actualizado correctamente.");
            ClearForm();
            await LoadAsync();
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            ShowError($"Error guardando rol: {ex.Message}");
        }
    }

    private void Edit(RoleDto role)
    {
        editingId = role.Id;

        formModel = new RoleFormModel
        {
            Code = role.Code,
            Name = role.Name,
            Description = role.Description,
            Permissions = role.Permissions,
            IsActive = role.IsActive
        };

        selectedPermissions = ParsePermissions(role.Permissions);
    }

    private async Task DeleteAsync(Guid id)
    {
        try
        {
            var response = await Api.DeleteAsync($"api/settings/roles/{id}?changedBy=admin-web");

            if (!response.IsSuccessStatusCode)
            {
                var error = await response.Content.ReadAsStringAsync();
                ShowError(error);
                return;
            }

            ShowSuccess("Rol eliminado correctamente.");
            await LoadAsync();
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            ShowError($"Error eliminando rol: {ex.Message}");
        }
    }

    private void ClearForm()
    {
        editingId = null;
        formModel = new RoleFormModel();
        selectedPermissions = new HashSet<string>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
    }

    private bool IsPermissionSelected(string code)
    {
        return selectedPermissions.Contains(code);
    }

    private void TogglePermission(string code, object? value)
    {
        var isChecked = value is bool boolValue && boolValue;

        if (isChecked)
        {
            selectedPermissions.Add(code);
        }
        else
        {
            selectedPermissions.Remove(code);
        }
    }

    private void ClearPermissions()
    {
        selectedPermissions.Clear();
    }

    private void SelectAdminPermissions()
    {
        selectedPermissions = permissionGroups
            .SelectMany(x => x.Permissions)
            .Select(x => x.Code)
            .ToHashSet(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
    }

    private void SelectReadOnlyPermissions()
    {
        selectedPermissions = permissionGroups
            .SelectMany(x => x.Permissions)
            .Where(x =>
                x.Code.EndsWith(".VIEW", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ||
                x.Code.EndsWith(".EXPORT", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ||
                x.Code.EndsWith(".DOWNLOAD", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ||
                x.Code.EndsWith(".EVENTS", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            .Select(x => x.Code)
            .ToHashSet(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
    }

    private void SelectOperationalPermissions()
    {
        var allowed = new[]
        {
            "DASHBOARD.VIEW",
            "INVENTORY.VIEW",
            "LOCATION.VIEW",
            "ASSIGNMENT.VIEW",
            "ASSIGNMENT.CREATE",
            "LIFERECORD.VIEW",
            "MAINTENANCE.VIEW",
            "MAINTENANCE.REQUEST",
            "MAINTENANCE.EXECUTE",
            "LOAN.VIEW",
            "LOAN.CREATE",
            "LOAN.DELIVER",
            "LOAN.RETURN",
            "DAMAGE.VIEW",
            "DAMAGE.REPORT",
            "PHYSICALCOUNT.VIEW",
            "PHYSICALCOUNT.EXECUTE",
            "DOCUMENT.VIEW",
            "DOCUMENT.UPLOAD",
            "DOCUMENT.DOWNLOAD"
        };

        selectedPermissions = allowed.ToHashSet(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
    }

    private static HashSet<string> ParsePermissions(string? value)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(value))
        {
            return new HashSet<string>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        }

        if (value.Equals("ALL", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
        {
            return new HashSet<string>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        }

        return value
            .Split(',', StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries | StringSplitOptions.TrimEntries)
            .ToHashSet(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
    }

    private void ShowSuccess(string value)
    {
        message = value;
        messageClass = "alert alert-success";
    }

    private void ShowError(string value)
    {
        message = value;
        messageClass = "alert alert-danger";
    }

    private sealed class RoleDto
    {
        public Guid Id { get; set; }
        public string Code { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string Name { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string? Description { get; set; }
        public string? Permissions { get; set; }
        public bool IsActive { get; set; }
    }

    private sealed class RoleFormModel
    {
        public string Code { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string Name { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string? Description { get; set; }
        public string? Permissions { get; set; }
        public bool IsActive { get; set; } = true;
    }

    private sealed class PermissionGroup
    {
        public string Area { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string Title { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public List<PermissionItem> Permissions { get; set; } = new();
    }

    private sealed record PermissionItem(string Code, string Name);
}

@rendermode InteractiveServer
@inject IHttpClientFactory HttpClientFactory

<PageTitle>Usuarios - Configuración</PageTitle>

<section class="users-tech-banner">
    <div>
        <span class="users-tech-pill">CONFIGURACIÓN</span>
        <h2>Usuarios</h2>
        <p>Crea, edita, activa o bloquea usuarios del sistema y asigna rol, sede y estado operativo.</p>
    </div>

    <div class="users-tech-side">
        <div class="users-tech-status">
            <span>Usuarios</span>
            <strong>@users.Count registrados</strong>
        </div>

        <a class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-light users-back-button" href="/settings">
            Volver a Configuración

        <h2>@(editingId is null ? "Crear usuario" : "Editar usuario")</h2>

            <DataAnnotationsValidator />

            <div class="mb-3">

                    <option value="">Todas / Sin sede</option>
                    @foreach (var branch in branches)
                    {
                        <option value="@branch.Id">@branch.Code - @branch.Name</option>
                    }
                </InputSelect>
            </div>

            <div class="form-check mb-3">
                <InputCheckbox class="form-check-input" @bind-Value="formModel.IsActive" />
                <label class="form-check-label">Activo</label>

        @if (isLoading)
        {
            <p>Cargando usuarios...</p>
        }

        {

                <thead>
                    <tr>
                        <th>Usuario</th>
                        <th>Nombre</th>

                        <th class="text-end">Acciones</th>
                    </tr>
                </thead>
                <tbody>
                    @foreach (var user in users)
                    {

                            <td><strong>@user.UserName</strong></td>

                            <td>
                                <span class="badge @(user.IsActive ? "bg-success" : "bg-secondary")">

                                <button class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-primary" @onclick="() => Edit(user)">Editar</button>
                                <button class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-danger" @onclick="() => DeleteAsync(user.Id)">Eliminar</button>
                            </td>
                        </tr>

    </div>

@code {
    private HttpClient Api => HttpClientFactory.CreateClient("NaviApi");

    private List<UserDto> users = new();
    private List<RoleDto> roles = new();
    private List<BranchDto> branches = new();
    private UserFormModel formModel = new();
    private Guid? editingId;
    private bool isLoading;
    private string message = string.Empty;
    private string messageClass = "alert alert-info";

    protected override async Task OnInitializedAsync()
    {
        await LoadAsync();
    }

    private async Task LoadAsync()
    {
        isLoading = true;
        message = string.Empty;

        try
        {
            users = await Api.GetFromJsonAsync<List<UserDto>>("api/settings/users") ?? new();
            roles = await Api.GetFromJsonAsync<List<RoleDto>>("api/settings/roles") ?? new();
            branches = await Api.GetFromJsonAsync<List<BranchDto>>("api/organization/branches") ?? new();
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            ShowError($"No se pudieron cargar los datos: {ex.Message}");
        }
        finally
        {
            isLoading = false;
        }
    }

    private async Task SaveAsync()
    {
        message = string.Empty;

        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(formModel.UserName) ||
            string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(formModel.DisplayName) ||
            formModel.AppRoleId is null)
        {
            ShowError("Usuario, nombre y rol son obligatorios.");
            return;
        }

        var request = new
        {
            userName = formModel.UserName,
            displayName = formModel.DisplayName,
            email = formModel.Email,
            position = formModel.Position,
            area = formModel.Area,
            appRoleId = formModel.AppRoleId.Value,
            branchId = formModel.BranchId,
            responsiblePersonId = (Guid?)null,
            isActive = formModel.IsActive,
            changedBy = "admin-web"
        };

        try
        {
            HttpResponseMessage response;

            if (editingId is null)
            {
                response = await Api.PostAsJsonAsync("api/settings/users", request);
            }
            else
            {
                response = await Api.PutAsJsonAsync($"api/settings/users/{editingId}", request);
            }

            if (!response.IsSuccessStatusCode)
            {
                var error = await response.Content.ReadAsStringAsync();
                ShowError(error);
                return;
            }

            ShowSuccess(editingId is null ? "Usuario creado correctamente." : "Usuario actualizado correctamente.");
            ClearForm();
            await LoadAsync();
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            ShowError($"Error guardando usuario: {ex.Message}");
        }
    }

    private void Edit(UserDto user)
    {
        editingId = user.Id;

        formModel = new UserFormModel
        {
            UserName = user.UserName,
            DisplayName = user.DisplayName,
            Email = user.Email,
            Position = user.Position,
            Area = user.Area,
            AppRoleId = user.Role?.Id,
            BranchId = user.Branch?.Id,
            IsActive = user.IsActive
        };
    }

    private async Task DeleteAsync(Guid id)
    {
        try
        {
            var response = await Api.DeleteAsync($"api/settings/users/{id}?changedBy=admin-web");

            if (!response.IsSuccessStatusCode)
            {
                var error = await response.Content.ReadAsStringAsync();
                ShowError(error);
                return;
            }

            ShowSuccess("Usuario eliminado correctamente.");
            await LoadAsync();
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            ShowError($"Error eliminando usuario: {ex.Message}");
        }
    }

    private void ClearForm()
    {
        editingId = null;
        formModel = new UserFormModel();
    }

    private void ShowSuccess(string value)
    {
        message = value;
        messageClass = "alert alert-success";
    }

    private void ShowError(string value)
    {
        message = value;
        messageClass = "alert alert-danger";
    }

    private sealed class UserDto
    {
        public Guid Id { get; set; }
        public string UserName { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string DisplayName { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string? Email { get; set; }
        public string? Position { get; set; }
        public string? Area { get; set; }
        public bool IsActive { get; set; }
        public RoleDto? Role { get; set; }
        public BranchDto? Branch { get; set; }
    }

    private sealed class RoleDto
    {
        public Guid Id { get; set; }
        public string Code { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string Name { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    }

    private sealed class BranchDto
    {
        public Guid Id { get; set; }
        public string Code { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string Name { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    }

    private sealed class UserFormModel
    {
        public string UserName { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string DisplayName { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string? Email { get; set; }
        public string? Position { get; set; }
        public string? Area { get; set; }
        public Guid? AppRoleId { get; set; }
        public Guid? BranchId { get; set; }
        public bool IsActive { get; set; } = true;
    }
}

    /* USERS TECH BANNER STYLE */

    .users-tech-status {

    .users-tech-status span {

                            <td class="text-end">
                                <button class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-primary" @onclick="() => Edit(warehouse)">Editar</button>
                                <button class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-danger" @onclick="() => DeleteAsync(warehouse.Id)">Eliminar</button>

@code {
    private HttpClient Api => HttpClientFactory.CreateClient("NaviApi");

    private List<WarehouseDto> warehouses = new();
    private List<BranchDto> branches = new();
    private WarehouseFormModel formModel = new();
    private Guid? editingId;
    private bool isLoading;
    private string message = string.Empty;
    private string messageClass = "alert alert-info";

    protected override async Task OnInitializedAsync()
    {
        await LoadAsync();
    }

    private async Task LoadAsync()
    {
        isLoading = true;
        message = string.Empty;

        try
        {
            warehouses = await Api.GetFromJsonAsync<List<WarehouseDto>>("api/settings/warehouses") ?? new();
            branches = await Api.GetFromJsonAsync<List<BranchDto>>("api/settings/branches") ?? new();
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            ShowError($"No se pudieron cargar los almacenes o talleres: {ex.Message}");
        }
        finally
        {
            isLoading = false;
        }
    }

    private async Task SaveAsync()
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(formModel.Code) ||
            string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(formModel.Name) ||
            formModel.BranchId is null)
        {
            ShowError("Código, nombre y sede son obligatorios.");
            return;
        }

        var request = new
        {
            code = formModel.Code,
            name = formModel.Name,
            description = formModel.Description,
            branchId = formModel.BranchId.Value,
            isActive = formModel.IsActive,
            changedBy = "admin-web"
        };

        try
        {
            HttpResponseMessage response = editingId is null
                ? await Api.PostAsJsonAsync("api/settings/warehouses", request)
                : await Api.PutAsJsonAsync($"api/settings/warehouses/{editingId}", request);

            if (!response.IsSuccessStatusCode)
            {
                ShowError(await response.Content.ReadAsStringAsync());
                return;
            }

            ShowSuccess(editingId is null ? "Almacén / taller creado correctamente." : "Almacén / taller actualizado correctamente.");
            ClearForm();
            await LoadAsync();
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            ShowError($"Error guardando almacén / taller: {ex.Message}");
        }
    }

    private void Edit(WarehouseDto warehouse)
    {
        editingId = warehouse.Id;

        formModel = new WarehouseFormModel
        {
            Code = warehouse.Code,
            Name = warehouse.Name,
            Description = warehouse.Description,
            BranchId = warehouse.BranchId,
            IsActive = warehouse.IsActive
        };
    }

    private async Task DeleteAsync(Guid id)
    {
        try
        {
            var response = await Api.DeleteAsync($"api/settings/warehouses/{id}?changedBy=admin-web");

            if (!response.IsSuccessStatusCode)
            {
                ShowError(await response.Content.ReadAsStringAsync());
                return;
            }

            ShowSuccess("Almacén / taller eliminado correctamente.");
            await LoadAsync();
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            ShowError($"Error eliminando almacén / taller: {ex.Message}");
        }
    }

    private void ClearForm()
    {
        editingId = null;
        formModel = new WarehouseFormModel();
    }

    private void ShowSuccess(string value)
    {
        message = value;
        messageClass = "alert alert-success";
    }

    private void ShowError(string value)
    {
        message = value;
        messageClass = "alert alert-danger";
    }

    private sealed class WarehouseDto
    {
        public Guid Id { get; set; }
        public string Code { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string Name { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string? Description { get; set; }
        public Guid BranchId { get; set; }
        public BranchDto? Branch { get; set; }
        public bool IsActive { get; set; }
    }

    private sealed class BranchDto
    {
        public Guid Id { get; set; }
        public string Code { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string Name { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    }

    private sealed class WarehouseFormModel
    {
        public string Code { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string Name { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string? Description { get; set; }
        public Guid? BranchId { get; set; }
        public bool IsActive { get; set; } = true;
    }
}

    private HttpClient Api => HttpClientFactory.CreateClient("NaviApi");

    private List<ZoneDto> zones = new();
    private ZoneFormModel formModel = new();
    private Guid? editingId;
    private bool isLoading;
    private string message = string.Empty;
    private string messageClass = "alert alert-info";

    protected override async Task OnInitializedAsync()
    {
        await LoadAsync();
    }

    private async Task LoadAsync()
    {
        isLoading = true;
        message = string.Empty;

        try
        {
            zones = await Api.GetFromJsonAsync<List<ZoneDto>>("api/settings/zones") ?? new();
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            ShowError($"No se pudieron cargar las zonas: {ex.Message}");
        }
        finally
        {
            isLoading = false;
        }
    }

    private async Task SaveAsync()
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(formModel.Code) ||
            string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(formModel.Name))
        {
            ShowError("Código y nombre son obligatorios.");
            return;
        }

        var request = new
        {
            code = formModel.Code,
            name = formModel.Name,
            description = formModel.Description,
            isActive = formModel.IsActive,
            changedBy = "admin-web"
        };

        try
        {
            HttpResponseMessage response = editingId is null
                ? await Api.PostAsJsonAsync("api/settings/zones", request)
                : await Api.PutAsJsonAsync($"api/settings/zones/{editingId}", request);

            if (!response.IsSuccessStatusCode)
            {
                ShowError(await response.Content.ReadAsStringAsync());
                return;
            }

            ShowSuccess(editingId is null ? "Zona creada correctamente." : "Zona actualizada correctamente.");
            ClearForm();
            await LoadAsync();
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            ShowError($"Error guardando zona: {ex.Message}");
        }
    }

    private void Edit(ZoneDto zone)
    {
        editingId = zone.Id;

        formModel = new ZoneFormModel
        {
            Code = zone.Code,
            Name = zone.Name,
            Description = zone.Description,
            IsActive = zone.IsActive
        };
    }

    private async Task DeleteAsync(Guid id)
    {
        try
        {
            var response = await Api.DeleteAsync($"api/settings/zones/{id}?changedBy=admin-web");

            if (!response.IsSuccessStatusCode)
            {
                ShowError(await response.Content.ReadAsStringAsync());
                return;
            }

            ShowSuccess("Zona eliminada correctamente.");
            await LoadAsync();
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            ShowError($"Error eliminando zona: {ex.Message}");
        }
    }

    private void ClearForm()
    {
        editingId = null;
        formModel = new ZoneFormModel();
    }

    private void ShowSuccess(string value)
    {
        message = value;
        messageClass = "alert alert-success";
    }

    private void ShowError(string value)
    {
        message = value;
        messageClass = "alert alert-danger";
    }

    private sealed class ZoneDto
    {
        public Guid Id { get; set; }
        public string Code { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string Name { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string? Description { get; set; }
        public bool IsActive { get; set; }
    }

    private sealed class ZoneFormModel
    {
        public string Code { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string Name { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string? Description { get; set; }
        public bool IsActive { get; set; } = true;
    }

@page "/technical-life-records"

<PageTitle>Hojas de vida técnicas</PageTitle>

<div class="page-header">
    <div>
        <h1>Hojas de vida técnicas</h1>
        <p>Consulta consolidada de hojas de vida digitales de herramientas y activos.</p>
    </div>
</div>

<section class="module-placeholder">
    <div class="module-placeholder-badge">Administración de activos</div>

    <h2>Módulo en construcción</h2>

    <p>
        Esta pantalla queda creada como punto de navegación del módulo <strong>Hojas de vida técnicas</strong>.
        El siguiente paso será conectar esta vista con API, reglas de negocio, permisos, reportes y flujos operativos.
    </p>

    <div class="module-placeholder-grid">
        <div>
            <span>Estado</span>
            <strong>Pendiente desarrollo funcional</strong>
        </div>

FILE: C:\Users\yquinto\OneDrive - Navitrans\Escritorio\Documentos\Herramientas\Herramientas&Activos\src\Navi.ToolsAssets.Admin\Services\Auth\WebAuthSessionService.cs
============================================================

namespace Navi.ToolsAssets.Admin.Services.Auth;

public sealed class WebAuthSessionService
{
    public bool IsAuthenticated { get; private set; }

    public string UserName { get; private set; } = string.Empty;

    public string DisplayName { get; private set; } = string.Empty;

    public string Role { get; private set; } = string.Empty;

    public string BranchCode { get; private set; } = "TODAS";

    public event Action? OnChange;

    public void Login(string userName, string displayName, string role, string branchCode)
    {
        IsAuthenticated = true;
        UserName = userName;
        DisplayName = displayName;
        Role = role;
        BranchCode = branchCode;

        NotifyStateChanged();
    }

    public void Logout()
    {
        IsAuthenticated = false;
        UserName = string.Empty;
        DisplayName = string.Empty;
        Role = string.Empty;
        BranchCode = "TODAS";

        NotifyStateChanged();
    }

    public bool HasRole(params string[] roles)
    {
        if (!IsAuthenticated)
        {
            return false;
        }

        return roles.Any(x => string.Equals(x, Role, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase));
    }

    private void NotifyStateChanged()
    {
        OnChange?.Invoke();
    }
}

FILE: C:\Users\yquinto\OneDrive - Navitrans\Escritorio\Documentos\Herramientas\Herramientas&Activos\database\scripts\001-create-database.sql
============================================================

IF DB_ID(N'NaviToolsAssetsDb') IS NULL
BEGIN
    CREATE DATABASE [NaviToolsAssetsDb];
END
GO

USE [NaviToolsAssetsDb];
GO

IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM sys.schemas WHERE name = 'Security')
    EXEC('CREATE SCHEMA Security');
GO

IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM sys.schemas WHERE name = 'Organization')
    EXEC('CREATE SCHEMA Organization');
GO

IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM sys.schemas WHERE name = 'Inventory')
    EXEC('CREATE SCHEMA Inventory');
GO

IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM sys.schemas WHERE name = 'LifeCycle')
    EXEC('CREATE SCHEMA LifeCycle');
GO

IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM sys.schemas WHERE name = 'Documents')
    EXEC('CREATE SCHEMA Documents');
GO

IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM sys.schemas WHERE name = 'Loans')
    EXEC('CREATE SCHEMA Loans');
GO

IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM sys.schemas WHERE name = 'Maintenance')
    EXEC('CREATE SCHEMA Maintenance');
GO

IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM sys.schemas WHERE name = 'Imports')
    EXEC('CREATE SCHEMA Imports');
GO

IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM sys.schemas WHERE name = 'Sync')
    EXEC('CREATE SCHEMA Sync');
GO

IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM sys.schemas WHERE name = 'Audit')
    EXEC('CREATE SCHEMA Audit');
GO

FILE: C:\Users\yquinto\OneDrive - Navitrans\Escritorio\Documentos\Herramientas\Herramientas&Activos\scripts\validate-dashboard.ps1
============================================================

$ErrorActionPreference = "Stop"

$apiBase = "http://localhost:5218"

Write-Host "Validando Dashboard NAVI..." -ForegroundColor Cyan

Write-Host "`n=== SUMMARY ===" -ForegroundColor Cyan
$summary = Invoke-RestMethod "$apiBase/api/dashboard/summary"
$summary | Format-List

Write-Host "`n=== HERRAMIENTAS POR ESTADO ===" -ForegroundColor Cyan
Invoke-RestMethod "$apiBase/api/dashboard/tools-by-status" |
    Format-Table status, statusLabel, count -AutoSize

Write-Host "`n=== HERRAMIENTAS POR SEDE ===" -ForegroundColor Cyan
Invoke-RestMethod "$apiBase/api/dashboard/tools-by-branch" |
    Format-Table branchCode, branchName, totalTools, availableTools, loanedTools, inMaintenanceTools, damagedTools -AutoSize

Write-Host "`n=== ALERTAS ===" -ForegroundColor Cyan
Invoke-RestMethod "$apiBase/api/dashboard/alerts" |
    Format-Table severity, internalCode, message -AutoSize

Write-Host "`n=== ACTIVIDAD RECIENTE ===" -ForegroundColor Cyan
Invoke-RestMethod "$apiBase/api/dashboard/recent-activity" |
    Select-Object -First 10 |
    Format-Table eventType, title, toolInternalCode, performedBy, eventDate -AutoSize

Write-Host "`nDashboard validado correctamente." -ForegroundColor Green
